Xu Mo reported on the significance of the meeting, followed by speeches by Xiao Wenshu, a representative of the Party Department, Zhong Shan, and Zheng Daode, a representative of the Railway Bureau. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 a.m. with slogans. (7th dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Hubei No. 3 Middle School Turmoil May Avoid Expansion

(Hankou) The turmoil at the No. 3 Middle School over rejecting the principal has been resolved by convening and guiding all teachers and staff, and expansion may be avoided. (7th dispatch)

Headquarters Orders Protection of Surrendered Red Bandits

(Hankou) The headquarters reordered the protection of surrendered Red bandits and strictly prohibits local bullies from seeking revenge. It also ordered the Pinghan and Hunan-Hubei railways to exempt connecting baggage from intermediate inspections. (7th dispatch)

Jia Shiyi Returns to Hankou from Nanjing

(Hankou) Jia Shiyi arrived in Hankou from Nanjing on the 7th and will go to the Department of Finance to take office. The administrative expenses of various agencies will be paid uniformly for the old year within the customs. (7th dispatch)

Guangdong to Abolish Export Tax on National Goods

(Guangzhou) The Guangdong Political Affairs Council passed the proposal to abolish the export tax on national goods on the 6th. (6th dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Luo Wengan to Leave Guangdong and Return North

(Hong Kong) Luo Wengan has completed his family affairs in Guangdong and is scheduled to leave Guangdong for Hong Kong on the 17th to wait for a ship to go north to cancel his leave. (7th dispatch from the Central News Agency)

Orders

On the 7th, the National Government ordered that He Jiwu, a supervisor of the Supervisory Yuan, who had requested to resign, should be relieved of his post. This is the order. The government also ordered that Du Chen be appointed as a supervisor of the Supervisory Yuan. This is the order.

The Current Situation of Japanese Immigration and Rural Decline

Changchun Correspondence: The most vigorous aspect of Japanese aggression in the Northeast today is the issue of immigration. Before the September 18th Incident, the number of Japanese who came to the Northeast was no more than 200,000, most of whom were employees of the South Manchuria Railway (SMR) and consulates. Japan's excuse of so-called overpopulation for immigration is merely a cover for international perception. After the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, in order to seize markets and sources of raw materials, the Japanese implemented their immigration policy with the mission of aggression. The Japanese Army Department, the Colonial Affairs Ministry, the Governor-General of Korea, and the SMR spent 100,000 yuan on investigation fees and organized the "Manchuria-Mongolia Immigration Investigation Committee." The Colonial Affairs Ministry also established the "Manchuria-Mongolia Immigration Bureau" to specialize in planning and implementing immigration. Since then, so-called "industrial immigrants," "fishing immigrants," "gold mining immigrants," and "armed group immigrants" have come in a steady stream. The number of Koreans crossing the river to the west is countless. It is difficult to count the numbers in remote areas. In major cities, Shenyang currently has more than 36,000 Japanese residents, an increase of 60% compared to before the incident. Harbin has about 8,000 Japanese residents, an increase of 45%. As for Changchun, the so-called "New Capital," it has about 4,400 Japanese residents, an increase of more than 27 times. This alarming rate of increase is only accelerating.

The Northeast's commerce has also undergone significant changes compared to the past. The Japanese monopoly on goods has reached perfection. European and American goods that were popular in the Northeast market in the past have disappeared today. Even Chinese products have suffered a fatal blow. For example, before the September 18th Incident, the Northeast market for porcelain was able to be self-sufficient with domestic products due to the protection of a high tax rate of 40%. Starting in July of last year (1933), the tariff rate was changed to 15% ad valorem according to the will of the Japanese. As a result, Nagoya porcelain products from Japan, which had once disappeared from the Northeast market, became very active and had the potential to dominate the Northeast market. Chinese products have since fallen into decline. Other examples include French silk fabrics, which have been overwhelmed by Japanese rayon, and German industrial machinery and pharmaceuticals, which have also been gradually eroded by Japanese goods. Therefore, the goods used in the Northeast today have almost become a Japanese monopoly. If one travels to major cities, one might as well be in a Japanese street. What one sees are Japanese people, and what one buys are Japanese goods. Advertisements for Japanese products are everywhere. The changes are lamentable. Last year, the Northeast had an unprecedented bumper harvest of soybeans, sorghum, corn, and other special products. The output was the highest in recent years. However, the result was not only not the "Manchurian development boom" as the Japanese claimed, but also a sharp drop in prices. It is expected that after the new soybeans appear, their prices will fall to half of what they were in previous years. The lives of farmers have been greatly affected, and bankruptcies are common, resulting in a so-called "famine in a year of plenty." The sharpness of the worldwide panic is one of the main reasons, but the following reasons are also responsible for this: (1) The most important special product of the bumper harvest is soybeans, and Germany, the consumer of soybeans and its products, has increased tariff barriers; (2) The puppet Central Bank has stopped purchasing special products; (3) The financial stagnation caused by the contraction of the puppet country's currency. The above reasons have caused the decrease in the export of special products and the tragic fall in prices, which in turn have led to a violent panic in the Northeast economy and have changed the Northeast's historically surplus trade into a deficit. The comparison with even the lower year of 1932 compared to last year is shocking. Here is a statistical excerpt:

Trade Volume in 1932 and 1933 (January to October) (Unit: 1,000 Yen)

| | 1932 | 1933 | Actual Increase/Decrease | Same Rate % |

| ------------- | --------- | --------- | ------------------------- | ----------- |

| Exports | 248,327 | 278,999 | Increase 30,672 | 12.3 |

| Imports | 157,359 | 296,302 | Increase 138,943 | 88.2 |

| Total | 405,686 | 575,301 | Increase 169,615 | 41.8 |

| Trade Balance | Surplus 90,968 | Deficit 17,303 | — | — |

The 1933 export item in the above table increased compared to 1932, but the speed of the increase was far less than that of imports, resulting in an unprecedented and terrible fact - a deficit. From another perspective, this deficit means that the bankruptcy of rural areas has accelerated. The puppet country authorities are therefore extremely anxious and embarrassed. In order to rescue rural areas on the verge of bankruptcy, they had no choice but to raise and lend 1,000 country yuan in "rural relief funds." Endo, the director of the puppet general affairs department, also announced the following countermeasures on December 30 of last year: (1) Adopt appropriate digestion methods to prevent this year's soybeans from being oversupplied; (2) Prevent price declines caused by farmers' eagerness to sell their products; (3) Reduce sales commissions, storage fees, railway freight, etc. to increase farmers' actual income. Based on the three major principles mentioned above, the following specific measures will be implemented by the agencies under the jurisdiction of the puppet Ministry of Industry, the puppet Ministry of Finance, and the puppet Ministry of Communications: (1) Under the subsidy of the puppet government, joint storage agencies will be established in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces, and the puppet Central Bank will expand the scope of financial accommodation for the storage of special products; (2) In addition to existing agencies, appropriate agencies will be established to guide the sale of special products; (3) Induce the complete elimination of a large amount of accumulated special products. While the puppet government authorities are providing relief to the Northeast rural villages on the verge of bankruptcy, in order to thoroughly eradicate the cause - the oversupply of special products - they are establishing so-called "joint sales associations" in Heilongjiang and other places. There is also a "Manchuria Special Products Central Company," which is intended to bring together all Manchurian producers, exporters, and shipping companies, which is also in the planning stages. According to the investigation, the content of this organization is attached below to show a glimpse. The "Special Product Loan Management Committee" of the same nature takes the provincial governor as the chairman. In addition to monitoring the joint sales association mentioned above, its duties include guiding the sale of soybeans and having international transportation companies be responsible for export and storage.

The joint sales association's measures are as follows: (1) Location and number: main distribution areas in northern Manchuria, namely 24 in Heilongjiang Province and several in Jilin Province; (2) Organization: Farmers within a certain area who need to entrust the storage and sale of soybeans must be members and must set up a chairman and representatives of the entrustors to handle association affairs; (3) Establishment fee: subsidized by the puppet government; (4) Business: According to the loan measures, accept the entrustment of the entrustor (borrower) and, with the consent of the entrustor, manage the following matters, namely joint storage, guarantee issuance, and joint sale of soybeans; (5) Calculation: The income and profit and loss of the sale of soybeans are shared jointly by all members according to the quantity of soybeans entrusted for storage; (6) Lending agency: Manchuria puppet Central Bank; (7) Loan amount: Farmers who have not yet received sufficient spring plowing loans can be granted an amount equal to 90% of the current price of soybeans within the total amount of principal and interest of the spring plowing loan, but half of the soybean loan must be paid into the puppet Central Bank as principal and interest repayment for the spring plowing loan; other farmers can be granted an amount equal to 70% of the current price; (8) Period: The maximum loan period shall not exceed three months, and if it is unavoidable, another proof may be established; (9) Interest: 7% per month. (January 25)

A Calamity for the Tianjin Business Community

Match Factories Unable to Sustain Themselves

Spinning Mills Plan to Cease Operations

Tianjin Correspondence: Last year, Tianjin, affected by the war, experienced instability and unrest in all aspects of society. In particular, the business community, with the blockade of the Hebei region, was unable to transport goods from the Northeast for sale. Consequently, the economic downturn was more severe than usual. Last year, the Ministry of Finance also issued new unified tax regulations, dealing another heavy blow to the business community, which had barely recovered. Since December, the match industry in Tianjin has been unstable, and now the fate of match merchants is hanging by a thread. It is known that there are only three match companies in Tianjin: Danhua, Beiyang, and Rongchang. Danhua has a capital of 1.7 million, Beiyang is divided into two factories, North and South, with a total capital of less than 300,000. Although Rongchang's capital is less than Danhua's, it is twice as large as Beiyang's. Normally, sales are influenced by dumping from the neighboring Shandong province. After the fall of the Northeast, sales in the war zone were also impossible. Most of the market share was taken by Japanese goods. Only southern Hebei and northern Henan can be relied on for support. With the increase in new taxes, the companies were not informed in advance, and the inventory could not be released to the market. Each company has an inventory of three to four thousand cases. In mid-December, they requested the Hebei Provincial Government and the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce to forward a request to the central Ministry of Finance for (1) exemption from the new unified tax and (2) permission to pay the old tax for the inventory of each factory before the issuance of the new unified tax order on December 5. However, repeated appeals were ineffective. The branch offices once expressed their intention to strike in protest, but were dissuaded by party and government agencies. From the beginning of December to late January, the factories agreed to pay the new tax, but due to sluggish sales, Danhua's inventory was 17,000 cases, Rongchang's 15,000 cases, and Beiyang's 11,000 cases, tying up a considerable amount of capital. Beiyang, with its weaker financial resources and the death of its general manager, lacked someone in charge, which led to financial difficulties. It first declared its inability to maintain operations. Half a month ago, the South factory stopped work. Later, due to the appeal of more than three hundred unemployed workers to party and government agencies for relief, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Committee reluctantly persuaded the factory to resume work. One party agreed to borrow 500,000 from the bank on behalf of the company. The three companies guaranteed the loan with their assets, and the funds were used to maintain operations. Beiyang South factory immediately resumed work. Just over ten days later, the party and government agencies failed to provide the promised loan. The company was forced to close down again the other day. The North factory has reduced its machinery and is temporarily struggling to survive. Although the party and government agencies know that this matter will have a great impact on the market, they are powerless to help and can only listen to it. Currently, the two agencies are negotiating the terms of dismissal with labor and management. The workers are demanding a month's wages as severance pay and travel expenses to return home. The company is still unwilling to agree, and the party and government agencies are trying their best to persuade them. Rongchang Company, amid the financial distress of Beiyang, struggled to support itself for a month. The other day, it also announced that its inventory was full and its working capital was exhausted. It submitted a report to the Municipal Government for permission to suspend work for a month from December 25th of the lunar calendar to sell its goods. If the inventory is sold out, it will continue to operate. Otherwise, it will shut down. The Party Bureau, believing that the financial distress of Beiyang alone was enough to shake the market, and that the failure of Rongchang would lead to more unemployment and increase social unrest, invited the manager of the company and representatives of the workers to the Municipal Government. The party and municipal agencies tried their best to persuade them. As a result, the workers' representatives agreed to work together with the company to overcome this difficulty. If wages cannot be paid in full, they can be reduced by a certain percentage, and then supplemented after the inventory is sold out. Rongchang, with no other option, agreed to comply. Danhua, with more available capital, is still able to maintain operations. It has not made any statement during the panic of Rongchang and Beiyang.

The crisis of the Tianjin match industry has been described above. The spinning industry is also in a precarious state. There are six companies in Tianjin: Huaxin, Hengyuan, Beiyang, Yuda, Baocheng, and Yuyuan. Yuda, established by the Japanese, has the most capital and its sales are uniquely broad due to raw materials. The other five companies are run by Chinese merchants. In the past, the sales of each company depended on exports to the Northeast. Last year, only Yuda, a Japanese yarn factory, could export to the Northeast. Hengyuan and Huaxin, along with the other five companies, were hindered by the high tariffs of the puppet regime. The sales of the five companies could only be promoted in the four provinces of Henan, Hebei, Chahar, and Suiyuan. As a result, sales were generally sluggish. Last year, Hengyuan and Beiyang, due to their weak financial resources, repeatedly threatened to collapse. They were only maintained with the utmost persuasion from party and government agencies. Recently, Hengyuan and Beiyang have reached the point of exhaustion and are unable to continue. They secretly sent people to report to the Municipal Party Committee, the Municipal Government, and the Social Affairs Bureau, planning to suspend operations within the lunar year. The two factories employ more than five thousand workers. If they close down, it will not only affect the market, but also make Huaxin and Yuyuan unable to maintain operations and successively declare bankruptcy. Therefore, the Municipal Government, in coordination with the Municipal Party Committee and the Social Affairs Bureau, summoned the managers of the two factories and urged them to maintain operations, taking the overall situation into consideration. The party and government agencies will try their best to find ways to coordinate loans with the banking community to get through the lunar New Year. The managers of the two factories, after being so earnestly advised by the authorities and promising relief, abandoned their plans to declare bankruptcy. However, with an inventory of more than two thousand pieces each, they plan to reduce the night shift after the lunar New Year to sell off accumulated goods. The party and government agencies, recognizing that this is a real situation, have allowed it. Therefore, the crisis of Beiyang and Hengyuan has been temporarily alleviated. The spinning and match industries are the main industries in Tianjin. Now that they are declining so drastically, it is also a misfortune for the economic business community of North China. (5th)

The Tibetan Situation After the Passing of the Dalai Lama

Internally Divided into Three Factions

Two Dalai Lamas Already Born in Eastern Tibet

According to the North China Daily News, a dispatch from Tachienlu on December 28th of last year stated that the news of the passing of the Dalai Lama only reached Tachienlu and the surrounding areas a few days ago via a telegram from Nanjing. Lamas and Tibetans here are now afraid that the spread of this news in Tibet may cause unrest. The Dalai Lama passed away on December 17th, but Tachienlu only learned of it on the 22nd. The cause of the unrest will likely come from three sources: (1) those who sympathize with the Panchen Lama and wish to see him reinstated; (2) those who sympathize with the current monastic regime and wish to see the clergy continue to hold power; and (3) the youth faction in Lhasa, who desire a strong political organization to control Tibet. The power of the youth faction is now growing daily. They aspire to make Tibet occupy a more important position among the nations. The Tibetan Transport Office, currently occupying the right bank of the Yangtze River opposite Tai Erji, is organized by this faction. These educated youths dislike the rule of the lamas and wish to implement a new political system in Lhasa. When the lama leaders go to seek the fourteenth Dalai Lama in the future, it is feared that each faction will show its power. Two Dalai Lamas have already been born in Eastern Tibet, one from Guotang and one from Gangda. This election will have significant political implications. Currently, there are 7,700 lamas and Gelugpa monks in Trilingben, most of whom come from Eastern Tibet. These people are inclined towards China. Sera has 5,500 lamas, and Galdan has 3,300 lamas, all of whom hold a neutral attitude. Trashilhunpo has 4,000 lamas and Gelugpa monks, who fully support their religious leader, the Panchen Lama. The large lama temples in Eastern Tibet are all inclined towards China and wish to see the Panchen Lama reinstated.

In the Midst of Shandong Party Affairs Disputes

Zhang Weicun Resigns

Personal Integrity Not Trusted

Internal Strife Within the Association

Jinan Correspondence: Shandong Province party affairs have been in dispute for many days and have not been resolved. Zhang Weicun, a Standing Committee member of the Provincial Executive Committee, has been the target of criticism by party members. Yesterday (the 5th), he sent a special telegram to Beijing to sincerely request resignation from his positions as member of the Provincial Executive Committee, Standing Committee member, and Anti-Corruption Commissioner. He requested that Han Fuju preside over the affairs of the Provincial Party Headquarters and that Lin Mingjiu, the Captain of the Special Service Team, be responsible for anti-corruption affairs. He also requested the Central Government to send someone to take over as soon as possible. The telegram stated: "I, Weicun, have been responsible for Shandong party affairs for several years. I have received guidance from the Central Government, assistance from local military and government officials, and the joint efforts of comrades in various counties. All elections have been handled in an orderly manner, and party affairs throughout the province have been smoothly advanced. However, since the election of representatives to the Fifth National Congress, the opinions of the Provincial Committee members have varied, leading to mutual stimulation and escalation. Eventually, all arrows were aimed at Weicun alone. During the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, some comrades even fabricated false accusations and publicly attacked Weicun. The Central Government's attempts to stop it were ineffective, and the situation has become increasingly amplified. In recent years, Weicun has only known to follow the instructions of the Central Government, do his best in his duties, and stabilize the local area. He has not been concerned with praise or criticism, gain or loss. Moreover, in recent years, the country has experienced many misfortunes, and the situation in Shandong Province is special. Even if Weicun cannot help the current difficulties, he should not burden the overall situation. Unexpectedly, personal integrity has not been trusted, and internal strife has occurred within the association, causing the previously stable local situation and harmonious party affairs to suffer adverse impacts. After introspecting, I am filled with shame and fear. After returning to Shandong, I actively concluded the various party affairs and anti-corruption tasks I was responsible for. However, two or three comrades in Beijing have fabricated rumors and are trying to harm me. Comrades in various counties, because Weicun has always been subject to slander, have gathered in the provincial capital and are planning to make some expressions. Weicun is deeply afraid that those who are misled will mislead the party. Therefore, I specially request to resign from my positions as member of the Shandong Provincial Executive Committee, Standing Committee member, and Shandong Anti-Corruption Commissioner, etc. I respectfully request that you approve this to avoid the path of the wise and quell rumors. All internal affairs of the association, with the exception of Committee Member Jiang Bocheng, who is in Peiping, the remaining four committee members are out of office in Beijing. Only Permanent Committee Member Han (Fuju) of this association in Jinan is requested to preside over everything to avoid interruption of association affairs. Regarding anti-corruption affairs, Captain Lin Mingjiu of the Special Service Team is temporarily responsible for maintaining order. Please send someone from the Central Government to take over as soon as possible. As for the points of attack against Weicun, in terms of party discipline, I will collect counter-evidence, compile it, and submit it to the Central Government to await disposition. In terms of national law, I will follow legal procedures to seek resolution. I respectfully submit this telegram for your consideration. Respectfully, Zhang Weicun, member of the Shandong Provincial Executive Committee, Standing Committee member, and Shandong Anti-Corruption Commissioner."

Jiangsu Province Compiles and Trains County Defense Corps

—Divides Each County into Three Classes and Determines the Number of Soldiers in the Teams According to Class—

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Jiangsu Provincial Government has already formulated unified establishment methods for the reorganization of the county police forces, and is now engaged in the compilation and training of county defense corps. The Security Department of the Civil Affairs Department has formulated implementation plans and detailed rules, focusing on the reorganization and establishment of temporary defense corps, the rules for methods, and the training of soldiers. It is also dividing the establishment of defense corps into two phases. The "First Phase" includes: Tongshan, Pi County, Suining, Suqian, Muyang, Donghai, Guanyun, Yancheng, Funing, Huaiyin, Lianshui, Siyang, Gaoyou, Nantong, Taixing, Rugao, Liyang, and Ganyu. The "Second Phase" includes: Dangshan, Xiao County, Pei County, Feng County, Huaian, Xinghua, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Yizheng, Baoying, Dongtai, Taixian, Qidong, Chongming, Haimen, Gaochun, Lishui, Jurong, Danyang, Jintan, Yangzhou, Wujin, Jiangyin, Wu County, Changshu, Kunshan, Wujiang, Songjiang, Qingpu, Jinshan, Fengxian, Chuansha, Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, Nanhui, Yixing, Jiangdu, Shanghai, and Jingjiang. Each county is required to establish a county defense corps headquarters by March 1st. The captains and other officers of the headquarters are to be filled by students from the military and police cadre training schools. The number of defense teams is determined by the population of each county. First-class counties establish two companies of Class A defense teams, training 1,188 regular soldiers each year. Second-class counties establish one company of Class A and Class B teams, and one company of Class B teams, training 918 regular soldiers each year. Third-class counties establish one company of Class A teams, training 594 regular soldiers each year. The expenses for first-class counties are more than 35,000 yuan per year, about 30,000 yuan for second-class counties, and 20,000 yuan for third-class counties. The following grades are divided according to the size of the population and the number of defense teams established. "First-class counties" are Zhenjiang, Kunshan, Wu County, Nantong, Rugao, Funing, Yancheng, and Tongshan. "Second-class counties" are Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Jinshan, Chongming, Haimen, Wuxi, Jingjiang, Taixing, Huaiyin, Huaian, Jiangdu, Dongtai, Xinghua, Taixian, Pi County, Guanyun, Qidong, and Suining. "Third-class counties" are Suqian, Muyang, Donghai, Lianshui, Siyang, Gaoyou, Liyang, Ganyu, Dangshan, Xiao County, Pei County, Feng County, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Yizheng, Baoying, Gaochun, Lishui, Jurong, Danyang, Jintan, Yangzhou, Wujin, Jiangyin, Changshu, Wujiang, Qingpu, Fengxian, Chuansha, Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, and Yixing. The implementation period is from May of the 23rd year. All required start-up costs and spring uniform costs are to be paid from the county's defense expenses, as decided by the 622nd meeting of the provincial government. In the future, after the establishment of the headquarters of each county's general team, district group deputy refresher training courses should be held to cultivate cadre talents. The soldiers are divided into three types: (1) Regular soldiers, with a service period of one year; (2) Reserve soldiers, with a service period of three years; (3) Rear reserve soldiers, with a service period of six years. (7th)

Songjiang

Re-election of the Xinzhuang Town Chamber of Commerce

The Huazhuang Town Chamber of Commerce in Songjiang County was established in the 32nd year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty and has been in existence for thirty years. After the promulgation of the revised organizational plan for people's organizations, six industries, including the rice industry, initiated the reorganization of the original chamber of commerce and obtained a permit from the Songjiang County Party Headquarters. A general meeting of all member representatives was convened on the first day of the past month, and executive and supervisory committee members were elected. Sixty-five people, including Wang Zhaoyun, attended the meeting on that day. Xu Zhao was sent by the County Party Headquarters to attend and provide guidance. Yang Tianduo, the District Chief of the Fourth District, was commissioned by the County Government to attend the meeting to supervise the election. As a result of the election, fifteen people, including Zhou Menglin, were elected as executive committee members, and seven people, including Xiang Changyan, were elected as supervisory committee members. The next day (2nd), the executive committee members mutually elected standing committee members and a chairman. As a result, Cheng Weiru, Jin Zhecheng, Shi Jiahang, Wang Zhaoyun, and Zhou Runqi were elected as standing committee members, and Wang Zhaoyun was elected as chairman. It has been reported to the Songjiang County Government and forwarded to the Industry Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government for filing.

Male Corpse Discovered on the Bund in Huangpu

An unidentified male corpse was discovered this morning in the area of Tu 19 on the Huangpu Bund outside the South Gate. It was determined that he had been shot and killed. The corpse was lying in the fields. The town police chief of the district, Lu Yunhai, reported the matter to the Procuratorate of the court for inspection. It is still being investigated who shot and killed the corpse. It is reported that the prosecutor has ordered the town police chief to obtain a coffin and prepare the body for burial, pending a public notice to claim the body.

Suzhou

The Jin Shuren Case is Prosecuted

Jin Shuren, the former Chairman of the Xinjiang Provincial Government, was regarded by all parties for his harsh administration while in office. He was subsequently detained in Beijing and sent to the Jiangsu Higher Court for trial. The Higher Court dispatched Prosecutor Kuang Bingqian to Beijing for interrogation, which has been concluded. After returning to the Higher Court in Suzhou, Jin was prosecuted in the same court based on the investigation results, which showed that Jin had committed acts of invading and occupying foreign lands, murdering, arson, and robbery. Yesterday (7th), Court President Lin Biao assigned the case to Judge Si Wen of the Criminal Division One and Lu Wenlan, Director of the Criminal Division Three, for trial. A date has been set for the trial to be held in Beijing.

The Main Culprit in the Wu Ta Township Robbery Case is Apprehended

Yang Renfu, a wealthy farmer in Wu Ta Township, Lu Mu District, Wu County, was shot and killed during a robbery last spring. The main culprit in the case, He Huaban A Jin, also known as Xu A Jin, was wanted by the authorities but had not been apprehended. Yesterday (7th), the Fourth Squadron of the County Police apprehended the Xu bandit at Yang Duantou, North-South Bridge, and escorted him to the city. According to his confession, he admitted to shooting and killing Yang Renfu and committing many other robberies. After being escorted to the county, he will be sent to the court for investigation.

A Death of Unclear Circumstances, Request to Open the Coffin for Examination

Mi Zhengxi, a leather craftsman from Sanliuwan, had a daughter named Lin Bao, who was fourteen years old. Due to her family's poverty, she was sold to Zhou Rulin's family as an adopted daughter at the age of six. Subsequently, Zhou was arrested and executed in Nanjing by Sun Chuanfang for the Duoshi case. Zhou's concubine remarried Liu Yueheng, the owner of the Daxingtai Hotel in Yao Family Alley. Lin Bao also went with her. Recently, Lin Bao died the other day due to being abused for a long time. According to neighbors, she was suffocated. Her father, Mi Zhengxi, came upon hearing the news and saw purplish marks on his daughter's chest. He believed that her death was unclear and requested the court to open the coffin for examination.

Changshu

Killing a Cat Causes a Major Disaster

In the Xingjiao Temple area of Tianzhuang Township, Benyi, there is a man named Gu Yuding, who has been teaching at the local Xingjiao Elementary School. His family is well-off and can live comfortably. The family kept a cat, which suddenly became wild the other day and snatched away two cured chickens from the house. Therefore, Yuding was extremely angry and thought of putting the cat to death. The next evening, he and his younger brother, Guiyu, waited for the cat to eat. They tied it up, poured kerosene all over its body, and set it on fire. After being set on fire, the cat cried out in pain, struggling desperately, so that the rope broke. It ran wildly and rushed into the firewood room. When Yuding and others saw this, they immediately tracked it down. Unexpectedly, in this dry weather, especially with firewood being prone to catching fire, the fire spread in an instant and could not be contained. They immediately rang the gong to warn the neighbors, but unfortunately, it was quite far from the town, and the village lacked fire-fighting equipment. It was too late to save the situation, so they let it spread. The neighbors were also affected. The fire was extinguished after burning for about three hours. It is estimated that more than 30 houses were destroyed, with losses of several thousand yuan.

Wuxi

Ministry of Transportation Convenes Shipping Conference

The Ministry of Transportation believes that China's shipping industry is still very young and needs to be promoted in terms of routes, tonnage, cooperative power, and business methods in order to develop. Therefore, it has decided to hold a discussion meeting at the Ministry on March 20 of this year to promote the shipping industry. Shipping associations and shipping companies from various places will each send two representatives to the Ministry to participate in the discussion on cooperation between shipping companies, promotion of domestic routes, and opening of ocean routes. Yesterday, the Ministry has sent letters of invitation and instructions to the shipping guilds of the various counties, ordering them to send representatives to Beijing to attend the meeting on schedule. The Wuxi Shipping Guild has received the order and has decided to send one representative from the guild, as well as one representative from the Xi Li, Xi Cheng, village barge, and freight barge. They are Chen Rongquan, Qian Weiqing, Chen Xiangqing, and Li Xuchu. The news has already been telegraphed to the Ministry.

Two District Chiefs Accused

Zhu Zhengxin, the District Chief of the 13th district in the county, was recently severely reprimanded by County Chief Yan for protecting gambling for forty-one days after County Chief Yan personally verified the evidence. The citizens of the district have also recently found out that District Chief Zhu has committed many bad deeds and have filed charges with the Party, government, and civil affairs departments. In addition, Hua Sigu, the District Chief of the 17th district, was recently accused by the residents of the district of (1) fabricating work reports, (2) undermining the regulations of the Yitu, (3) embezzling public funds privately, and (4) abusing his power and employing private individuals. A petition has been filed with the Civil Affairs Department requesting his removal.

Farm Woman Gives Birth to Three Strange Children in a Row

Wu Guisheng, a villager from Miaoqiao near Huangtutang in the Seventh District (HuaiShang City), is in his thirties and works as a farmer. His wife gave birth to a son several years ago, but the child had no anus on his buttocks and vomited filth from his mouth. He died within a few days. Wu Guisheng and his wife were misled by superstition and burned the child's corpse. The following year, they gave birth to another boy, but unexpectedly, he still had no anus. Wu Guisheng and his wife were very angry and buried the child in the fields. To their surprise, the other day, they gave birth to another boy, still without an anus. Although they tried to pierce it with a candle, it had no effect. Wu Guisheng placed the child in the wilderness and set it on fire at 2 p.m. yesterday, but the child did not cry, only made a sound like a chick. He died soon after. It is said to be strange.

Robbers Rob and Injure People in a Row

You Abao, a villager in Xitianzhu Alley, Si Tou Town, Fifth District, is approaching the age of knowing fate and has some land. He has children under his knees. Unexpectedly, around 3 a.m. yesterday, four robbers suddenly came, each holding a sharp blade, and entered by digging a hole from the back door. They tied up the victim and warned him not to make a sound, forcing him to tell where the silver was hidden. You Abao resisted slightly and was beaten fiercely with fists and feet. Then they searched separately and robbed him of silver dollars, clothes, etc., totaling more than 50 yuan. The robbers were still not satisfied and broke into the door of You Ayuan's house next door and searched arbitrarily. They robbed him of clothes, jewelry, silver dollars, etc., worth about 300 to 400 yuan. The victim has now issued a list of losses and reported the robbery to the 13th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. In addition, the Xishan News Agency in Luhua Alley outside the North Gate was burglarized around 2 a.m. yesterday (7th). The thieves entered through the window from the river bank at the back door and stole the clothes, silver dollars, etc. of the president and reporters of the agency, worth about dozens of yuan. Separate reports have been filed with the County Bureau requesting investigation.

Changzhou

Robbers Commit Robbery and Kill Two People

On the night of the 5th, around 11 p.m., more than ten robbers suddenly came to the home of Shi Huihui, a villager in Shijiajiao Village, Guan'an Township, Third District, Wuyi, and entered the room to commit robbery. Shi's younger brother, Hua Da, fled out of the door and was shot and killed by the bandits. Shi Huihui then sneaked out of the house and rushed to report to the District Chief Chen Yi, asking him to send a team to arrest the bandits. District Chief Chen immediately led the defense corps to go there. Unexpectedly, they encountered the bandits in the area behind the Hanjia Village in Handi. The bandits immediately opened fire to resist arrest, causing Wu Xifu, an investigator at the district office, to be shot and killed. The corps soldiers then opened fire to fight back. After holding out for about an hour, the bandits were unable to hold on and fled in all directions. In addition to sending a team to go to the Donghenglin Qishuyan Railway Station to pursue the bandits, Chen Ou reported the matter to the county government on the 6th, asking them to order the arrest, and also notified the county court to send someone to the village to examine the corpses. In another message, District Chief Chen was also shot and injured while leading the team to pursue the bandits. The county government, believing that the bandits were rampant, has strictly ordered the police to arrest them and bring them to justice.

Local News

Last Year's City Population Statistics

Over 3.3 Million People

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau has achieved significant results since handling household registration investigations. The "January 28th Incident" in the previous year caused difficulties in household registration investigations in Shanghai due to various reasons. The bureau made great efforts to rectify the situation, and it has now become normal, with various investigation reports being submitted monthly. However, after the "January 28th Incident," the population in the city suddenly decreased. It was not until last year that it gradually increased. The total population in the last month of the previous year was 339,585 households with 1,662,711 people. By the last month of last year, the number of households had increased to 377,332, and the population had increased to 1,846,178. The total population of the city is uncertain because it is impossible to carry out investigations in the special districts. According to the police department of the special district, the survey in October of the 19th year and September of the 22nd year shows that there are 971,397 Chinese and 36,471 foreigners in the Public Concession, and 478,755 Chinese and 17,781 foreigners in the French Concession. Together with the city, the total population is about 3.3 million.

Last Year's Import Surplus of 700 Million Yuan

Detailed Investigation by the International Trade Bureau

Complete Investigation Expected by Mid-Next Month

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, the market conditions in various countries were sluggish throughout the past year, and countries have built high tariff barriers against each other to seek resistance. Therefore, foreign goods have flooded the Chinese market, resulting in a shocking increase in imports last year. Due to the sluggish industrial and commercial conditions in our country, exports have not increased. According to Mr. He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, the total value of foreign goods imported last year was about 1.3 billion yuan, while the value of exported goods was only about 600 million yuan, resulting in an import surplus of 700 million yuan. Among the imported goods from various countries, the United States accounted for the largest share, followed by Britain, Japan, and Russia. Other countries such as Germany, France, Poland, Belgium, and Sweden were also involved. The detailed statistics and the number of imports from each country are currently being drafted by the International Trade Bureau, and the statistical report is expected to be completed by mid-next month.

The Pu An Steamer and a British Merchant Ship

Collided in the Huangpu River Yesterday

The Bow of the Pu An Damaged

The Forecastle is Cracked and Flooded

The British Ship's Midships is also Damaged

Public Inspection Today

The China Merchants Bureau's Qingdao Class Steamer Pu An was robbed last time, and the case has not yet been solved. The steamer came to Shanghai from Qingdao yesterday and entered the Huangpu River. When it reached within the Wusong Estuary, it collided with the British merchant ship Philoctetes of the Blue Funnel Line. The bow of the Pu An was completely damaged, and the outer hull of the Blue Funnel Line's midships was also damaged. Both ships have berthed at the wharf and will be inspected by the impartial personnel requested by both parties today to determine the responsibility. The details are as follows:

The Pu An Arrived in Shanghai from Qingdao. The China Merchants Bureau's Pu An Steamer sailed from Qingdao to Shanghai, carrying many goods and passengers. Yesterday afternoon at 1 o'clock, the steamer arrived at Wusong and immediately entered the Huangpu River, preparing to dock at the Hua Zhan Wharf in Pudong to unload goods and passengers. Captain Rex, First Mate Sun Zuoren, and others were all on duty on the bridge, carefully navigating. At 1:05, the Pu An sailed in front of the Zhabei Power Plant when it suddenly collided with the Philoctetes, a giant steamer of the Blue Funnel Line, causing a major accident. Both ships were damaged.

Two Ships Collided in the Huangpu River. The British merchant ship Philoctetes of the Blue Funnel Line transported goods to Shanghai from Liverpool. After unloading a part of the goods in Shanghai, it was heading to Dalian, Japan, and other places yesterday afternoon. When it sailed to the river surface in front of the Zhabei Power Plant, it was close to the Pu An Steamer, and both should have given way. According to Mr. Zhao Yuntai, Director of the Shipping Department of the China Merchants Bureau, the Pu An and the British ship were trying to avoid each other, resulting in carelessness, which caused the hulls of the Pu An Steamer and the Philoctetes to suddenly come close to each other. Unable to avoid, a violent collision occurred.

Conditions of Injuries on Both Sides. During the collision, the bow of the Pu An Steamer and the outer hull of the left midships of the British ship Philoctetes collided violently. The captains of the two ships immediately reversed their engines. At this time, the left side of the bow of the Pu An Steamer was dented by the British ship, and the keel of the bow was also broken. At the waterline of the bow, the iron plate was broken and a large hole was torn, and the forecastle was flooded with water, causing significant damage. The outer iron plate of the midships on the left side of the British ship Philoctetes was also damaged. The degree of damage was slightly less than that of the Pu An because the midships was fully loaded with goods, so the damage was also not insignificant.

Personnel Dispatched to the Ship for Inspection. After the accident, the Pu An immediately sailed to Hua Zhan to berth, and the British ship also stopped exporting and sailed back to the Blue Funnel Wharf. Each dispatched crew members to report to the company. The China Merchants Bureau received the report at around 2 o'clock in the afternoon. Zhao Yuntai, Director of the Shipping Department, along with engineers Zhang Yao and Huang Zonglun, took a small steamer to Pudong to board the Pu An Steamer for inspection and inquired about the cause of the accident from Captain Rex. The damaged areas were verified and recorded by engineers Zhang and Huang. As for the collision situation, there is a relationship of responsibility, so it will be determined after the public inspection by the notary today. It is inconvenient to announce at this time.

Reported to the Shanghai Harbor Master. The China Merchants Bureau has reported this matter to the Customs Harbor Master, and the Blue Funnel Line has also reported to the Shanghai Taipan by its shipowner and submitted it to the Harbor Master for inspection. The passengers of the Pu An, which came to Shanghai from Qingdao, immediately went ashore as scheduled and were sent to the new customs wharf by a small steamer to disembark. The cargo inside the ship was unloaded as usual. Zhao Yuntai, Director of the Shipping Department, and engineers Zhang and Huang, who inspected the ship, returned to the bureau at 6 o'clock in the evening and reported to General Manager Liu that night.

Public Inspection Together Today. Regarding the responsibility for the collision between the two ships, as well as the degree of damage and the losses of both parties, the China Merchants Bureau and the Blue Funnel Line have reported to the marine insurance companies and will jointly hire impartial personnel to inspect the two ships today, and inquire about the sailing conditions of the two shipowners and how the collision occurred, so that the impartial personnel can determine the responsibility.

Pu An's Earlier Suspension for Repair. According to Director Zhao, the Pu An Steamer was originally planned to be suspended for repairs during the upcoming Chinese New Year holiday because the furnace needed to be repaired. Now that the collision has occurred, the steamer must be suspended earlier and towed into the dock for repairs after the impartial person verifies it today.

Shanghai Harbor Sees Hungarian Ship for the First Time

First Time Since Trading with European Countries

According to the Zi Lin Newspaper, yesterday marked the first time since China began trading with European countries that a Hungarian ship, the Oriental, entered Shanghai Harbor. The ship was originally the British ship Tetriqitan, with a net tonnage of 2,722 tons and a displacement of 8,000 tons. It was purchased by its current owners a year ago. Although it is registered in the Hungarian capital, it cannot sail there because its size prevents it from entering the Danube River. Except for the seven Arab stokers, all the crew members are Hungarian. This time, it set sail from the Port of Sulina in Romania on the Black Sea with 7,500 tons of wheat, passing through Columbus and Singapore, and arriving in Shanghai after a voyage of 55 days. It is currently berthed at the China Merchants Bureau East Wharf and is unloading goods. It will stay in Shanghai for at least ten days before sailing to Dalian, where it will load soybeans. According to the ship's First Mate Inno, there are a total of five Hungarian sea ships. The Abata sank in the Indian Ocean a month ago, and only four remain. After the European War, two-thirds of Hungary's land was divided among other countries and newly formed countries according to treaties. Its only seaport, Fiume, was also lost. Therefore, although the ships fly the Hungarian flag, they cannot meet with their motherland.

The Money Trade Association Decided in the General Meeting

Annual Closing Method

Regulations on Interest Collection, Ticket Time, and Interest Spreads

Four Days of Holiday from the 14th to Organize Everything

The money trade industry set February 13th as the end of the 22nd year. The Money Trade Association held the fourth member representative meeting of the second session in the Ningbo Road Association Hall the day before yesterday, chaired by Qin Runqing, to propose a case on handling business before and after the total closing of the 22nd year, and requested a public decision. After discussion by all the representatives present, the following was decided: (1) The total closing period of the 22nd year was decided to be February 13th, from the 14th to the 17th as a four-day holiday after the total closing to organize everything, and during these four days, it will be the dismissal period. (2) Regarding the interest issue before the total closing, it was decided that by February 8th, the deposit interest will be deducted according to two yuan, the outstanding interest will be added according to four and a half yuan, and from February 9th, the outstanding interest will be added according to four and a half yuan. (3) Additional deposit ticket current fund, it was decided that there is no need to add deposits this year. (4) During the ticket collection period, it was decided that February 8th, 4 pm will be the deadline, and the return of tickets will also be delayed by one hour as usual, and tickets will be resolved as they come on the 13th. (5) Interest spread, it was decided to open until February 12th.

Former Secretary of the Xinjiang Provincial Government

Zhong Ying Talks About the Reasons for the Rebellion in Southern Xinjiang

It is Not Easy to Use Troops There

The Future Cannot Be Ignored

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the news of the independence of Southern Xinjiang has been confirmed by all parties. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency specifically visited Mr. Zhong Ying, former secretary of the Xinjiang Provincial Government, to inquire about the details. The details are as follows:

Reasons for the Rebellion. According to Mr. Zhong, he has been away from the south for a long time, so the recent situation is extremely isolated. However, in the past, the Han Chinese of Kashi were absolutely obedient to the orders of the provincial government, so they were at peace. There are very few Han Chinese in the area, and the Han Chinese all believe in Islam, so they are all Muslims. However, most of these religious people are engaged in business. In addition, there are the Kirgiz, who are also a type of Han Chinese. On the border of Afghanistan and Soviet Russia, there is another tribe that is usually the same as the Mongols, accustomed to nomadic life, and more hardy. Therefore, during this rebellion, there were Kirgiz soldiers who once occupied the Han city and carried out massacres before withdrawing. The reason is unclear, but it is suspected that the reason for this rebellion is that they took advantage of the fact that Xin's chaos could not be taken care of, and took the opportunity to change.

It is Difficult to Use Troops. However, if troops are used, the most difficult thing is the matter of supplies. Kashi is very far from the provincial capital, and the transportation is very inconvenient. If you travel by horse-drawn carriage, it will take a month to arrive. There are two routes from Dihua to Shufu, one via Dihua to Kuqa and the other via Dihua to Turpan, separated by the Tarim Basin (i.e., the Great Gobi). The area is a desert and cannot be used for military operations. Taking a detour, the journey is long and difficult. Therefore, although this incident is very simple in fact, it cannot be viewed vaguely. What is to be feared is that its actions may have a background, and the authorities have the difficulty of being beyond their reach. The only important thing at present is to hope that the central government has a quick solution, then the suppression will be easier. Otherwise, the longer the night, the more dreams there will be, and the future cannot be ignored.

Page 12

Increase in Kerosene Tariff

The City Chamber of Commerce Cables a Request for Postponement

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance yesterday, (omitting the title) that on the 6th of this month, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce's branch telegram opened, reporting that the Ministry of Finance instructed the Chief Inspector of Customs to open a brief statement: "The current import tax on kerosene (including other mineral oils for lighting) is levied at 0.1137 gold units per unit, and the tax on gasoline (including various unnamed engine fuels) is levied at 0.47 customs gold per unit, which will be implemented from February 1st, 23rd year," etc. It is verified that kerosene is a necessity for the daily use of ordinary people, and gasoline is the motive power of machines, and is especially important for the lifeline of industry and transportation. Taking Su La oil as an example, the original price was 70 yuan per ton, but it soared to 50 yuan in just a few days. At this time, when the social economy is becoming increasingly bankrupt, the impact on the daily use of ordinary people is not small. According to legislative procedures, increasing the tax rate must be approved by the Legislative Yuan to take care of people's livelihood and show caution. Now, according to the requests for relief from the wheel boat, water pumping, and rice milling machinery industries in our county, we have always known that your association leads the merchants, and the whole country admires it. In addition to telegraphing the central government to order the Ministry of Finance to withdraw the order, we also ask for consistent advocacy. At the same time, according to the Shanghai Inland River Steamboat Industry Association's branch telegram, it is briefly stated that members have recently come to the association to say that the engines installed on the bureau's steamboats are all suitable for thin juice diesel as fuel. Eight years ago, the price was only more than 40 yuan per ton, and it has gradually increased over the years to 74 yuan and 30 cents. Unexpectedly, recently, the Ministry of Finance believes that this thin juice diesel can be refined into kerosene for lighting, and the tariff is increased by 26.30 gold units per ton, which is about 50 yuan in national currency. The previously established kerosene refining management regulations stipulating that imported diesel must be guaranteed by merchants to be used for refining kerosene were abolished, so that the Mobil and other companies also skyrocketed the price of this oil by 50 yuan per ton. In this way, the necessary supplies used by the bureau's steamboats are suddenly taxed by the Ministry of Finance to 70% of the original price, creating a new precedent for heavy taxes. In name, it increases the import tax on foreign merchants, but in reality, it absorbs our people's fat and blood. The bureau's steamboat merchants are unable to bear this unreasonable heavy tax, and have sent a special letter requesting that you quickly transfer the matter to the City Chamber of Commerce to petition the government to immediately cancel it for relief, etc. Based on this, it is verified that the above-mentioned sections are all true. The inland river boat industry is in a precarious situation. I念that our government authorities should vigorously maintain the Three People's Principles. According to the previous situation, we dare to appeal to your association to ask for orders for the merchants and to telegraph the Ministry of Finance, that for this case, it should be treated reasonably and exempt from being included in the crude oil for refining, so as to avoid the extra heavy taxes that航商should not bear. Etc. to the association. Based on this, it is verified that a separate standard for classifying and taxing imported diesel and kerosene has been approved by the Jianghai Customs and forwarded for announcement. The Inland River Steamboat Industry Association immediately based its voice on this announcement, and the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce still bases itself on the sections reported in the newspaper. Although the basis is different, the purpose of the request is the same. Now, because of the tax increase, the price will rise accordingly, and the impact on industry and people's livelihood is not small. It is reasonable to report the situation and ask your ministry to review it and give an order to postpone the implementation of the tax increase agreement to show leniency. In anticipation of the imminent telegram, Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce respectfully kowtows. Fish seal.

Public Security Bureau Orders Subordinates

Do Not Illegally Detain Suspects

Turn Over to the Courts Within Two Hours

Violators Will Be Treated as Unauthorized Imprisonment

Wen Hong'en, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, due to frequent illegal detentions of suspects by his subordinates, has specifically stipulated that all suspects must be handed over to the detention center for custody within two hours. The following is a record of his instructions: It is hereby ordered that all subordinate units must comply. Upon investigation, it has been found that various departments under this bureau, when handling cases and arresting suspects, often delay in handing them over to the courts for interrogation, resulting in an unclear accumulation of prisoners in the detention center, as well as deaths due to illegal detention of suspects. Human rights are at stake, and the reputation of the police is at stake. Although the bureau has issued transfer slips to save time in transferring cases, delays still occur, which is highly inappropriate. In the future, all units must adhere to Article 1 of the Supplementary Regulations of the Detective Team and hand over suspects to the courts for interrogation within three hours of their arrest. Delays are not allowed. Furthermore, when various departments request the interrogation of suspects, they must notify the Third Section beforehand, unless they have a handwritten order from the bureau director, in order to comply with procedures and avoid confusion. In addition to separate orders, Article 1 of the Supplementary Regulations of the Detective Team is hereby copied and issued for compliance. This order is issued on February 5th, the 23rd year of the Republic of China by Bureau Director Wen Hong'en. Attached is Article 1 of the Supplementary Regulations of the Detective Team: If the detective team arrests any suspects while handling cases under orders, they shall be handed over to the detention center for custody within two hours and a written statement of the case shall be sent to the Third Section for review. A report shall also be submitted to the bureau director. The deadline shall not exceed three hours. Violators will be treated as unauthorized imprisonment.

German Egg Tax Has Been Ordered to Be Negotiated

There are currently no plans to revise the Sino-German Customs Treaty. Revisions to Paper Classification and Valuation

Chinese Cotton Mills Are Unlikely to Be Optimistic This Year

Revitalizing Rural Areas Is the Fundamental Solution

Japanese Yarn Dumping Deals a Heavy Blow to Us

According to news from the cotton yarn industry, the production and sales situation of yarn mills in various regions last year has been distributed in the form of a survey table by the National Federation of Chinese Cotton Mills, but it has not yet been collected. However, based on the general situation, although the resistance of Shanghai's yarn mills is stronger, Japanese merchants are actively expanding and competing, which will deal a heavy blow to us. The situation this year is still unlikely to be optimistic. The following is a record of what they said:

Few Factories Made Profits Last Year According to the discussion, the federation conducts surveys of production and sales in various regions every year in order to audit the situation of the national yarn industry within a year. Various survey tables have now been issued, but some factories still adhere to conventions and settle accounts at the end of the old lunar year, so the summary table has not yet been collected and calculated. However, based on the general situation, very few factories were able to make profits last year. High cotton prices, low yarn prices, dumping of foreign goods, and social unrest in various regions have all dealt a heavy blow to yarn mills. The factories in Shanghai have stronger resistance, so they can still maintain operations. Those in Tianjin, Hankou, and Qingdao have even suspended work due to excessive inventory.

Relief of Yarn Prices Can Only Treat the Symptoms Although yarn prices have risen recently, by about four yuan per bale, cotton prices have also risen, by five yuan per dan. Therefore, calculated by cost, the price increase still results in losses. Moreover, since the September 18th Incident of the year before last, wars have continued in various parts of the country, the market has been depressed, and commerce has stagnated, which has had a huge impact.

Japanese Merchants' Steps to Invade Me The most powerful foreign competitor is Japan. Its plan this year is to add factories in Qingdao and expand spindles in Shanghai. The Japanese yarn industry's invasion of us in the fifteenth year was to develop in the interior. Therefore, at that time, yarn mills were established in various ports along the Yangtze River. Later, due to the difficulty of coping with incidents in various locations, it has recently changed again and concentrated its development in Shanghai and Qingdao. Shanghai is located at the mouth of the Yangtze River and can control the entire basin, making it the source of its competition. Qingdao is an important port in Shandong Province and can control North China, making it the tail end of its dumping. Therefore, the yarn industry in our country in the 23rd year is still not optimistic.

International Trade Association Requests

Reduce Tax Rate on Goods Transported to France

Comments on the Petition Table to Adelman

Hoping France Will Reduce Tax Rates on Our Country's Goods

Shen Shi News, this city: Adelman, Vice President of the Paris International Trade Association, previously sent a petition table to promote Sino-French trade and requested that two Chinese representatives be appointed to participate in the International Trade Association. The Paris International Trade Association held a meeting last year. The International Trade Bureau forwarded the order from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to select representatives. However, due to the proximity of the meeting, it was not possible to send personnel. This time, the association sent a petition table and again requested that representatives be appointed. The Consul General in Paris intends to appoint Lu Qinzai and Ma Shoubai as representatives to attend the meeting nearby. The ministry ordered the Trade Bureau to forward the request to the Chamber of Commerce and the China International Trade Association for reply. According to inquiries by the Shen Shi News reporter, the China International Trade Association agrees with the Consul General in Paris's intention to have Lu and Ma represent it at the meeting. As for the items mentioned in the petition table of the Paris International Trade Association, the association has considered them in detail and has prepared opinions to be forwarded to the National Trade Bureau for reference. Excerpts of its opinions are as follows:

Advocating Maintaining the Current Tax Rate (Above Omitted) Regarding the association's (referring to the Paris International Trade Association, hereinafter the same) request to reduce the tax rates on French specialty industrial products, such as wool yarn, woolen fabrics, cloth, printed cloth, raw silk fabrics, rayon fabrics, perfumes, cosmetics, lace, champagne, high-grade brandy, and cheese, etc., it is noted that customs duties are divided into fiscal taxes and protective taxes. The purpose of fiscal taxes is to enrich the national treasury, and the height of their tax rates is naturally limited. The purpose of protective taxes is to protect domestic industries and resist foreign competition, and the intention of their tax rates is naturally different from fiscal taxes. However, they should also take into account the interests of consumers and not exceed the necessary limit. Moreover, if the tax rate is too high, smuggling is inevitable, and administrative expenses will expand accordingly, which may result in more harm than good. Since our country's tariff autonomy, the tax rates on wool yarn, woolen fabrics, cloth, silk fabrics, rayon fabrics, perfumes, cosmetics, and cheese have indeed increased compared to the old tax rates. However, these goods either have luxury characteristics, or although they are not luxury goods, they are not French specialties. Due to the most-favored-nation clause in our country's customs treaties, if the tax rate on these French imports is reduced, similar products from other countries will also benefit, which may not be possible at present. This association believes that maintaining the current tax rate for a considerable period of time is a compromise that takes both sides into account.

Supporting the Reduction of Rayon Tax Regarding the association's request to separately stipulate the tax rates for raw silk and rayon, and that rayon is a daily necessity and should not be taxed too heavily, it is noted that rayon is a raw material for fabrics, and our country does not currently produce it. Its tax rate should not be compared with that of natural silk, and it should be levied at a lower rate. In the past, rayon was taxed at 5% of its value, but in 1929, it was increased to 10% of its value. Calculated at the prices at that time, it was equivalent to a tax of more than 10 taels per dan. In the 1931 tariff, it was changed to a specific tax of 58 gold units per dan. Since August 1932, it has been raised again to 73 gold units per dan, which is equivalent to more than 80% of its value. The tax rate cannot be said to be high. The import tax on rayon in India is only 25% of its value, and in Japan it is 101 Japanese yen per 100 catties, which are all lighter than in our country. Since the successive tax increases, the import volume of rayon has tended to decline year by year, and smuggling is rampant, which has harmed legitimate merchants. The association's statement on reducing the import tax on rayon is feasible from both the perspectives of developing domestic industries and expanding the national treasury.

Trademark Rights and Interests Are Not a Problem Regarding the association's request to protect trademark rights and the original names of various commodities, such as champagne, brandy, and cheese, it is noted that Article 6 of our country's Trademark Law stipulates that "Foreign nationals who wish to exclusively use their trademarks in accordance with treaties on the mutual protection of trademarks shall apply for registration in accordance with this law." Therefore, French imports that have been registered can be protected by law, which is not a problem.

Export Agencies Should Be Abolished as Soon as Possible Regarding the association's request to reduce the taxes on various important Chinese exports, it is noted that taxing export goods will increase the cost of domestic products and reduce their competitiveness in the international market. In modern times, except for a few special monopoly exports that are still taxed, most countries not only exempt taxes on general goods but also provide subsidies. Our country's international trade has long been in a deficit position. In recent years, due to the loss of a part of the trade in the three northeastern provinces and the impact of the global economic recession and the increase in tariff barriers in various countries, the amount of the deficit has intensified. In 1932, it reached more than 500 million yuan, and in 1933, it reached more than 700 million yuan. The future is dangerous beyond words. Export taxes should be abolished as soon as possible as a remedy after the fact.

Hoping France Will Give Preferential Treatment to National Goods It is noted that international trade aims to facilitate the exchange of goods, and customs duties should be based on the principle of reciprocity, which is beneficial to both parties. The French side requests that our country reduce import taxes, and this association expresses its strong support. However, at the same time, it is hoped that France can also give corresponding preferential treatment to our country's exports. It is noted that the Sino-French Customs Treaty stipulates that the Chinese goods that enjoy the lowest tax rate include pure silk fabrics, pure silk scarves, pure silk crepe, pure silk nets, pure silk lace, pepper, chili, cinnamon, whole and shelled nutmeg, cloves, and tea. However, the large-volume goods exported to France, such as eggs and egg products, peanuts, raw silk, raincoats, straw hat braids, pig intestines, pig bristles, tung oil, cowhide, and antimony, have not been explicitly included in the lowest tax rate, which undoubtedly hinders the promotion of Sino-French trade. This association hopes that the association will understand this situation and propose to the French government that the above-mentioned goods be allowed to apply the lowest tax rate, which will greatly benefit the progress of trade between the two countries. (Below Omitted) It is heard that the association's opinion letter has been sent by the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce to the International Trade Bureau and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and will be forwarded by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Paris International Trade Association for reference, so as to promote trade between the two countries.

Water Price Research Association

Meeting Today to Solicit Opinions from All Parties

The Real Estate Association Sends Kui Yanfang to Attend

Since the Shanghai British Concession Water Company changed the block-rate water system to a meter system, disputes have repeatedly arisen between tenants and landlords. This is because the rents in the Public Concession vary greatly between the central areas and the remote areas. Moreover, the residents in the remote areas are mostly laborers. In a single house, it is often divided into five or six households, and the water consumption is higher than in the central areas. Previously, when the water fee was charged at 7.5% of the rent, the burden was very light. Now that the water fee is paid according to the meter system, the difference is huge, so the landlords refuse to pay, resulting in the tragedy of water being cut off. In order to study and resolve the above-mentioned disputes, the Public Concession Bureau of Works has specially formed a Water Price Research Committee, inviting Feng Bingnan, Mei Jiufu of the Bureau of Works, and Canna, the manager of the Mobil Oil Company, to be committee members on the Chinese side. In order to solicit opinions from all parties, it has been decided to convene the chairman of the Western Real Estate Association and the chairman of the Shanghai Real Estate Association to attend the meeting at 3:00 p.m. today to submit opinions for adoption. Kui Yanfang has been designated to attend on behalf of the Real Estate Association, and a letter was sent to the association yesterday, stating: We have received your letter and are respectfully informed that Mr. Kui Yanfang has been designated to represent this association at the meeting of your committee at 3:00 p.m. on the 8th of this month. We hope that you will take note of this.

Kidnapping, Theft, and Bandit Crimes Sentenced

Fan Xiaomei, a young woman from Gaoyou, 19 years old, recently came to Shanghai from her hometown and lived in a bungalow in Xinjiamu Bridge, Hongkou, intending to find work in a yarn mill. She was tricked by her fellow villagers Zhang Baocheng and Zhang Zirong to go to New World for entertainment between December 19th of last year. Later, they went to the Hongyun Hotel at 564 Haining Road and prevented her from going out. They colluded with Zhou Hailin, who was at large, and planned to sell her to a man surnamed Li for 190 yuan to be his wife. However, the matter was discovered by Chinese Detective Xu Yongyuan of the Hongkou Police Station, who secretly went with a Western detective and arrested the two Zhangs. After interrogation, it was learned that Zhang Zirong had also committed theft with his accomplice Chen Haiqing from Jiangbei, who was hiding at 762 Lafayette Road in the French Concession. The detectives went again and arrested Chen, along with the bill of sale, and brought them to the police station. Fan Xiaomei was claimed by her family. After investigation, it was found that Zhang Zirong and Chen Haiqing had committed armed robbery with accomplices between September and December 5th of last year, robbing the households of Yuan Cao, 42 Xinzha Road, Tan Wang, 1007 Roberts Road, Cao Yunming, 1485 Yuyuan Road, and Zhao Kenzai, 1035 Jinsheng Road, of valuables worth more than 1,300 yuan. They were sent to the First Special District Court, but Zhang Zirong only admitted to one case of theft. They were ordered to await sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui came to the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Zhang Baocheng to two years of imprisonment, Zhang Zirong to four years of imprisonment, and Chen Haiqing to nine years of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the final judgment will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. The bill of sale was confiscated. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Bureau of Works, stated that the defendants had also committed theft and robbery in the Chinese territory. The Public Security Bureau sent detectives to the court today to transfer them, but the Yulin Road Police Station also had robbery cases committed by these people. It is necessary to investigate them in detail. Please postpone the transfer. Judge Liu approved this and informed Detective Chen Guiqing of the Municipal Public Security Bureau.
