Detectives Bravely Fired Bullets Like a String of Beads

One Thief Shot Dead, One Thief Captured

Robbery in Yihe Alley, North Chengdu Road Last Night

Three Thieves Came Together, Resulting in Only One Thief Escaping

- Random Bullet Injured Two Passersby -

Since the beginning of winter in this city, theft cases have occurred frequently in various places, even several times a day. Fortunately, the city's police organs have spared no effort in pursuing and arresting them, so the detection of cases is also very rapid. However, a group of people who are willing to violate the law and take risks is like this. Therefore, if the residents' door and window security is slightly careless, they will be taken advantage of. At 6:30 p.m. yesterday, when a certain family at No. 48, Yihe Alley, North Chengdu Road, was having dinner, three bandits suddenly broke into the back door. One bandit guarded the back door, one bandit and one bandit with a gun went straight into the inner room, shouted at everyone, forbade them to make a sound, and watched them. At the same time, they forced the victim to hand over the keys, and the unarmed bandit went to each room to search, rummaged through boxes and cabinets, and looted almost everything. All the jewelry and cash were looted in large quantities. After about half an hour, they left after a full looting and fled in the direction of South Chengdu Road. When the victim saw this, he chased out anxiously and shouted to catch the robbers. The nearby patrol officers heard the news and immediately fired their guns and chased after them, blowing their whistles madly. At this time, the Chengdu

Road Police Station also got the news and urgently dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to cooperate in the pursuit. When the bandits saw this, they fled urgently in the direction of Chenjiabang Small Vegetable Market. However, at this time, the Chinese and Western detectives had also arrived. The bandits were in a hurry, so the bandit with the gun fired a shot. At this time, the detectives also fired their guns at the same time, and bullets like a string of beads were shot at the bandits. One of the bandits fell to the ground in response and was shot dead on the spot by the detectives. Before long, one bandit was also injured and captured. However, there was still one bandit who escaped. At the same time, two passersby, Liu Jinrong from Nanjing, 25 years old, and Cai Ronggen, a local, 23 years old, were injured by stray bullets because they happened to be passing by during the fierce battle and did not have time to avoid them. Liu was injured in his left shoulder, and Cai was grazed by a bullet. They were all sent to Renji Hospital for treatment by Western Police Car No. 231. The injured bandit was escorted back to the police station. After a brief interrogation, he was transferred to the hospital for treatment because he had suffered serious injuries. He will be dealt with according to the law after he recovers. At the same time, the accomplices who escaped are being pursued. The body of the dead bandit will be reported for autopsy this morning. The amount of losses suffered by the victim is not known in detail.

This Year's Solar Eclipses to Occur Four Times

According to news from the Xujiahui Observatory in this city, there will be two solar and two lunar eclipses this year: (1) Solar eclipse: The first will be a total solar eclipse on February 14th (i.e., the Lunar New Year's Day). The path of totality will pass over the South Pacific Islands and the Pacific Ocean. A partial eclipse will be visible in parts of China.

The eclipse will begin at approximately 7:00 AM, reach its maximum at 7:48 AM, and end at 8:40 AM. The second solar eclipse will be an annular eclipse on August 10th. The path of annularity will pass over South Africa, and it will not be visible in China. (2) Lunar eclipse: The first already began on January 30th at 11:59 PM, reached its maximum at 0:40 AM on the 31st, and ended at 1:22 AM. The second will begin on July 26th at 6:52 PM, reach its maximum at 8:13 PM, and end at 9:34 PM.

Yangtze River Water Recedes Again

Wuhu: 7 feet 9 inches

Unprecedented Shallow Water

All Ships of Six Companies are Hindered

The current low water level of the Yangtze River is rarely seen in previous years. At the lowest point, the downstream water level receded to 8 feet 9 inches, causing all Yangtze River steamers to be stopped. On the 5th of this month, the Jianghan Customs announced that the waterway south of Madang was one foot and four inches deeper than the original Laogang channel, allowing steamers to pass. Unexpectedly, by the 6th, the water level in the southern channel had again dropped to 9 feet 8 inches. Contrary to expectations, the water level in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River receded even further yesterday, reaching a record low that has never been seen before. Even ships of around 1,000 tons cannot pass. The situation is being investigated and reported as follows:

(Significant Drop in Downstream Water Level) This time, the low water level in the Yangtze River first appeared in Wuhu and then moved to Madang Port near Xiaogushan. The water level in that section was only 8 feet 9 inches at its lowest, causing Yangtze River boats passing through to either run aground or scrape the bottom. Just as the shipping industry was overjoyed that the southern channel was open to Shanghai, the water level unexpectedly dropped after only one day, though ships could still manage to sail. Unexpectedly, the water level in the downstream Wuhu area fell drastically today, reaching an unprecedented low of only 7 feet 9 inches, a record low for the Yangtze River.

(Report from Wuhu) Yesterday at noon, the Shanghai Sanbei Steamship Company received an urgent telegram from its Wuhu branch stating that since the night of the 6th, the water level in the Wuhu area of the lower Yangtze River had dropped sharply. The shallowest point is now only 7 feet 9 inches, which is shallower than the Madang Laogang water gauge. Not only can larger steamers not pass, but even third and fourth-class ships can hardly navigate. Generally, the smallest type of Yangtze River boat requires a draft of at least eight feet when empty, unless it is a shallow-water-class ship from the upper reaches.

(Ships of Various Companies Hindered) A few days ago, when Madang had shallow water, the Yangtze River steamers of the six companies in Shanghai could still reach Anqing to unload cargo and passengers, using small tugboats to pull them through the mud. Now that the water level in Wuhu has dropped to 7 feet 9 inches, the upstream ships of the various companies, even when empty of cargo and passengers, can hardly be towed through. They can only send barges from both upstream and downstream to transship cargo, turning the Yangtze River steamers into connecting vessels halfway. The Jing'an, the Sanbei Company's ship with the shallowest draft, was also reported by the Wuhu branch yesterday to be unable to pass through this shallow section.

(Losses During the Low-Water Period) This time, the low water level in the Yangtze River has blocked both the upper and lower reaches. The reporter met with Director Wei and Mr. Lao of the Jiejianhua Company today. They said that last year, the various shipping companies on the Yangtze River line suffered business losses, and last month, they were hindered by the low water level. The grounding of Yangtze River steamers on the upper and lower reaches and the delays caused by the blockage of all the steamers affected no fewer than fifty or sixty ships. Each ship lost an extra four or five hundred yuan for each delay of two days per trip. Since the water level receded, it has been three weeks. Some Yangtze River steamers have run aground, while others have been stranded en route. The shallow-water fees charged by the shipping companies are hardly enough to cover the cost of tugboats and small laborers. In total, the losses from the low water level of the Yangtze River over the past twenty days are truly shocking. Now that the water level in Wuhu has dropped to 7 feet 9 inches, the shipping companies are suffering even greater losses.

Municipal Government Staff

Establish a Cooperative Society

Capital of $5,000 to Start a Restaurant

Mayor Wu and Yu Hongjun Elected as Directors

The personnel of various agencies under the Shanghai Municipal Government have established a cooperative society to handle consumer affairs. The circular and regulations are recorded below:

The Secretariat of the Municipal Government issued a circular to all staff members of the Municipal Government, requesting them to participate in the cooperative. The circular stated that the Municipal Government staff members have organized a cooperative society to handle consumer affairs, with a fixed capital of $5,000, divided into 1,000 shares, each share costing $5 silver yuan. The first subscription meeting was held on January 22nd, and it was decided that the society would begin operations when one-quarter of the capital had been subscribed. This amount has now been fully subscribed, and it has been decided to formally establish the society. Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yu, and Secretary Tingrong have been elected as directors for this term to carry out the work. It has been found that most of the members are from our office. The staff of your bureau are also colleagues and should be encouraged to participate enthusiastically. Therefore, we have enclosed the society's constitution and sent it to you. Please inform the staff of your bureau that those who wish to join the society should contact Secretary Zhang Tingrong directly.

Constitution of the Cooperative Society: The constitution of the cooperative society states: (1) The staff of the Shanghai Municipal Government are organizing a cooperative society to handle consumer affairs. (2) The society's fixed capital is $5,000, divided into 1,000 shares, each share costing $5 silver yuan. The society will begin operations when one-quarter of the shares have been subscribed. (3) Anyone who invests $5 or more in the society will be a shareholder and have one vote. (4) All staff members of the Municipal Government may join as shareholders of the society. Upon leaving the job, their shares will be repurchased by the society at a price determined by the society, or they may be taken over by other staff members of the Municipal Government. Those who do not wish to transfer their shares may retain them. (5) The society will first start by opening a restaurant and gradually expand to sell household clothing, appliances, and utensils. (6) The society will have three directors, who will be elected by the shareholders for a one-year term. They will serve without pay. (7) The society will have one manager, who will be responsible for handling business operations. The manager will be appointed by the directors and will serve without pay. (8) The manager may hire staff as needed for business operations, but must obtain the permission of the directors in advance. (9) The manager will have one voluntary accountant, who will be appointed by the directors. (10) The society's accounts will be settled daily and reported monthly. One director will be appointed as an auditor to review and approve the accounts. (11) The society's operating surplus will be handled by the board of directors in accordance with the provisions of Article 12, and the plan will be submitted to the shareholders' meeting for resolution and implementation. (12) At the end of the year, if the society has a surplus, after deducting depreciation, the official profit will be deducted first, limited to 10% of the total capital. If there is a further surplus, it will be divided into ten parts: five parts for dividends, three parts for public reserve funds, and two parts for remuneration for the persons in charge. (13) Official profits will be distributed according to the number of shares. Dividends will only be enjoyed by shareholders who are also customers and will be distributed according to the total amount of money paid for goods by each individual in the current year. (14) The shareholders' meeting will be held every six months and convened by the directors. A quorum will be at least one-half of the total number of shareholders, and a majority of those present will be required for a vote. (15) Shareholders have the right to submit written proposals to the shareholders' meeting, but they must be submitted ten days before the meeting. In the event of important matters, a special shareholders' meeting may be convened at the request of one-third or more of the shareholders. (16) This constitution may be amended with the consent of two-thirds or more of the shareholders present at the shareholders' meeting.

The "Stealing the Sky and Swapping the Sun"

Loan Scam Exposed

Where Did the Paste Come From?

The Judge Saw Through Everything

Cheng Gongyuan, residing at No. 54 Yu Kang Li, Pi Shao Nai Road, French Concession, previously engaged in the jewelry business. In 1923, he was introduced by a friend to the Star Film Company and became acquainted with his colleague, Shen Guozhen. Later, Cheng returned home to care for his sick father. During that time, Shen Guozhen often visited Cheng's home for casual conversation. Cheng noticed that Shen was wearing a high-quality military uniform and asked Shen about his official position. Shen replied that he was a military officer and encouraged Cheng to enter politics, offering to help him find a position. Cheng was deeply grateful. Later, Shen said that if he succeeded in finding a position for Cheng, Cheng would need to pay a reward. Cheng voluntarily agreed to pay 500 foreign dollars if the matter was successful. At that time, a note was written and given to Shen to take away. Unexpectedly, Shen brought the note to Cheng the next day, saying that the reward was too vague. He had prepared a draft that was changed to "payment upon obtaining the position" and asked Cheng to sign it. Cheng thought it was reasonable and signed the note, adding his seal. From that day on, there was no news. Cheng assumed that Shen had not succeeded in finding him a position. Until March of 1932, Cheng suddenly received a letter from a lawyer entrusted by Shen, urging him to return a diamond ring weighing one carat, three gold bracelets weighing four taels each, and fifty pearls worth seven yuan each, for which Cheng had written a loan note. Cheng stated that he had not borrowed anything and denied it through his lawyer. However, Shen Guozhen filed a lawsuit in the Second Special District Court. Cheng Gongyuan read the loan note in court and confirmed that the signature was indeed his. He was speechless and unable to defend himself, resulting in a loss in the case and a judgment to repay the current value. However, after the judgment, Cheng was unwilling and tried to figure out what had happened. He realized that he had written a note entrusting Shen to find him a position, and because the scope was not specified, Shen Guozhen wrote a draft note and asked him to sign it. He must have realized that this was the source of the trouble. Therefore, he hired lawyer Ge Zhitan to appeal to the Third Branch of the Higher Court. The court session was held a few days ago, and Judge Guo Dezhang and Investigator Li attended the court. The appellant, Cheng Gongyuan, carefully examined the signature area of the loan note and noticed traces of paste next to it. He then realized that the note Shen Guozhen had brought to be replaced was a layered piece of patterned paper. After the appellant signed and sealed it, the upper layer was removed and the false note was arbitrarily written. Judge Guo questioned the appellee, Shen Guozhen, as to why there were traces of paste around the signature area of the loan note. Shen claimed that he did not know. Judge Guo believed it was a case of fraud and forgery. The debate was then concluded, and the date for the verdict was set for yesterday. Judge Hao announced the main text of the verdict, overturning the original judgment. The appellee's request for the previous portion was dismissed, and the costs of the two lawsuits were borne by the appellee. The case is called "Great Exposure."

Did the Mother Secretly Murder Her Own Grandson?

The Truth of the Family Matter Must Be Thoroughly Investigated

Chen Zhang, a woman from Gaoyou, is 61 years old and has two sons. The elder son is named Erhai (30 years old), and the younger son is Erzhu (24 years old). Wang also works in a yarn factory. The family's finances are quite comfortable. This year, around the autumn of the lunar calendar, Chen Zhang came to Shanghai with her younger son, Yizhu, due to famine in their hometown, and lived with her elder son and his wife. Erhai handed over the management of the family's finances to his mother. Erhai's wife, Wang, was very unhappy and told her father, Wang Hengyuan, (who lived nearby) who repeatedly used excuses to pick quarrels with Chen Zhang, even teaming up with his younger sister, Xiao Qiaolian, (22 years old) to make Zhang miserable. Because she had no way to live in her hometown, she endured the abuse and barely survived. On the night before last (the evening of the 5th), at 4 o'clock, the wicked daughter-in-law Wang murdered the grandson. The wicked daughter-in-law actually harmed her own grandson, which is extremely cruel. Yesterday, Chen Wang and her younger sister Xiao Qiaolian were arrested and detained by the police at the First Precinct of the Fifth District. She is requesting an examination of the body and asking for the wicked daughter-in-law to be severely punished. Subsequently, after a preliminary hearing by the prosecutor, the order was given to wait for the examination before a decision could be made.

According to the Guowen News Agency, various Muslim organizations in this city recently received a telegram from the Nanchang City Mosque and Qingzhen Elementary School in Jiangxi Province, stating that since the people of their religion have always adhered to a policy of isolation, adhering to old customs internally and lacking publicity externally, people outside the religion do not understand the content of religious doctrines. There are often those with a smattering of knowledge who fabricate groundless rumors and write insulting things. Recently, they saw that the Nanchang Guangyi Bookstore was selling "The Romance of the Fragrant Concubine" published by the Shanghai Jingzhi Bookstore. The book was published in 1926, and the editor was a Mr. Hu. It is not known which province he is from. Moreover, the book is priced very cheaply, and many people are buying it. It is rumored that the copyright has now been resold to the Shanghai Guangyi Bookstore for distribution in various provincial capitals. We still hope that in the future, attention will be paid to the novels and literature sold by bookstores in various provinces, counties, and major ports. All books of the Canon of Islam published by our Islamic religion can still be displayed in various libraries for non-Muslims to browse from time to time, so as to serve as propaganda. The above methods can prevent insults in the future. The telegram is urgent, and we are filled with anticipation. It is reported that after receiving the telegram, the various Muslim organizations in this city are currently discussing how to negotiate.

Zhenjiang-Danyang-Jintan-Liyang Long-Distance Buses

Joint Transportation with the Jinpu Railway

Effective from March 1st

The Zhenjiang-Danyang-Jintan-Liyang long-distance bus route runs from Zhenjiang via Danyang to Jintan (the section from Jintan to Liyang is not yet open to traffic). The company submitted a request last year to arrange joint transportation with the Jinpu Railway and requested a stop on the road at Danyang Station. The Traffic Department of the two railways sent personnel to discuss the joint transportation arrangements, and the Engineering Department ordered workers to fill in the pond at Danyang Station to facilitate the company's stop. The joint transportation contract and procedures have recently been approved and formally signed by the administrative bureaus of the two railways and will take effect on March 1st. The following is a summary of the contract: The Railway Bureau will sell joint tickets at six stations: Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Shanghai. Before the company completes the entire route, it will temporarily sell joint tickets at Jintan Station. Other stations can be gradually expanded with the agreement of both parties when needed. Danyang will be the connecting station for both parties. The Railway Bureau will provide transportation according to the class specified on the ticket, while the company will not differentiate between classes. The validity period of the joint transportation ticket will be two days. If the train is delayed by 15 minutes or less, the company will wait for the original bus. If the delay exceeds 15 minutes, the company will use a special bus to transport the passengers according to the number of passengers. The company's operating hours are from 6:55 AM to 5:11 PM daily. The Railway Bureau's joint transportation station will not sell joint tickets for any train that cannot reach Danyang Railway Station by 4:10 PM. The company can sell joint tickets during operating hours, except for night buses. If the operating schedule needs to be modified, both parties must notify each other in advance. In addition to passenger buses, the company is equipped with luggage trailers to transport joint transportation luggage and packages. All freight charges will be collected from passengers.

A Bomb Hidden in Bread

Thugs Intimidate Zheng Qiuting

Initially Demanding a Huge Sum of 30,000 Yuan

- Detectives Negotiate on Behalf and Arrest Two Thugs -

Zheng Qiuting, a Chaozhou native, also known as Shaoqiu, courtesy name Kejun, lives at No. 10 Meifu Lane, Parker Road. He runs the Fa Ji Coal Company and the Parker Road Yongyuan Pawnshop in Hankou Road, and his business is booming. He has accumulated a lot of wealth, which has attracted the attention of bandits. On February 6th of this year, Zheng suddenly received a threatening letter delivered by mail, signed by the "Blood Soul Assassination Squad," which stated that Zheng had previously engaged in drug trafficking in the Tianjin area and made a huge profit. The squad was short of funds and requested Zheng to provide substantial assistance in order to protect his business interests. Zheng ignored the letter. Later, the bandits repeatedly threatened him by phone, demanding 30,000 yuan. Zheng continued to stall with empty words. On the morning of the 4th of this month, a rectangular loaf of bread was suddenly found in the middle of the small gate outside Zheng's house. The servant handed it to Zheng, who examined it carefully and saw a round bomb in the middle of the bread, with a threatening letter attached. The letter accused Zheng of deliberately delaying and refusing to pay the ransom, and warned him with an attached explosive device. The letter demanded that Zheng quickly send 30,000 yuan to the fields near the new Shanghai Municipal Government in Jiangwan. The person delivering the money should carry a calendar as a sign. Zheng was shocked and immediately went to the Xin Zha Police Station in his jurisdiction to report to the head of the police. He immediately ordered Western Detective Chief Li Te, Chinese Detective Chiefs Tang Jian and Yao Yuanlong, Detectives Su Yinggen and Yang Peizhang, Detectives Yang Yunfeng and Xia Yeshan, etc., to investigate. In addition to taking the bomb and the previous two threatening letters back to the police station to prevent danger, he also ordered detectives to stay at Zheng's house and maintain strict vigilance. On the morning of the 5th, the telephone at Zheng's house rang loudly. The detectives on duty answered the call. It was indeed the bandits calling to inquire if there was any sincerity in negotiating. The detectives replied that there was indeed sincerity, but the ransom was too large and the negotiation location was too far away in Jiangwan, making it inconvenient to travel back and forth. They requested to change the location and reduce the ransom. The two sides negotiated for a long time on the phone. The bandits gradually reduced the ransom from 30,000 yuan to several thousand yuan, and the detectives also deliberately haggled. They initially agreed to several hundred yuan, then increased to one thousand yuan, but still without result. So they agreed to continue the discussion at a later time. Unexpectedly, at 8 p.m., the bandits called again. The detectives answered the call again. After a brief discussion, the amount gradually approached an agreement. As a result, it was agreed to meet at the entrance of the Yuegong Restaurant on North Sichuan Road from 3 to 4 p.m. on the 6th, still using a calendar as a secret sign. After obtaining the exact address, the detectives reported to the head of the police, who ordered trusted detectives to disguise themselves and go to the scene to wait on time. He also sent a detective to pretend to be Zheng's representative, carrying a calendar in one hand and a paper package in the other, pretending to be several thousand yuan in cash, and wandering around the Yuegong Restaurant. At 3:30 p.m., two bandits, Chen Dimin and Chen Xiangyao from Jiangsu, arrived. Xiangyao stood in the middle of the road as a lookout, while Dimin stepped forward and spoke to the detective pretending to be the representative. At that moment, the detectives swarmed forward and arrested the two Chens and took them to the police station. Subsequently, Chen Dimin led the detectives, together with detectives from the Public Security Bureau, to No. 7 Xingaoyang Lane, Qimei Road, Zhabei, where they confiscated many pieces of iron used to make bombs and took them back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First District Court. Police Lawyer Jiang Baolian rose to explain the circumstances of the case and requested a postponement in order to continue the investigation. After Judge Xue Lanru interrogated Zheng Qiuting and the two defendants, he ordered Chen Dimin and Chen Xiangyao to be remanded in custody pending further questioning at a later date.

Mailing Morphine Discovered

At around 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, a package from Guangdong and Hong Kong addressed to You Ting Ji in Shanghai arrived at the Wenjiaqiao Postal Branch in West Shanghai. The addressee, Wang Mingxing, a Sichuan native residing at No. 89 Run'an Lane, West Gate Road, French Concession, was sent to the branch to collect it. After the postal worker retrieved the package, he discovered that there were hidden items inside. Upon opening the package, he found a bag of morphine weighing 175 grams. As the matter concerned the private mailing of prohibited drugs, the branch immediately sent the witness and the package to the Sixth District Sub-Station in Zhoujiamei, and then transferred them to the Sixth District Police Bureau. After interrogation by District Officer Xing, the bureau prepared a document and sent it back to the branch for handling.

Zhou Exuan and Zhang Zhuying Lawsuit Awaits Re-Examination

Zhou Exuan, the eldest son of Zhou Weishi, the owner of Zhou Geng Ji Yarn Shop, a wealthy Suzhou merchant in Shanghai, had a brief affair with the famous prostitute Hong Lou Lao Si (i.e., Zhang Zhuying) ten years ago, and had a son named Dayuan. After his parents found out, they dissolved the small family he had formed, and the two lovers separated. However, Dayuan was still raised by Zhang, with Zhou responsible for the ______________. After Zhou stopped paying living expenses seven months ago, Zhang, on behalf of her son, sued Zhou ______________ in the First Special District Court. The case has already been heard once. Because Zhou denied it, he was ordered to summon witnesses to prove the facts. The case has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Guo Xiangzu opened the court for further hearing. The two witnesses, Fang Chen and Liu Wu, both complied with the summons and appeared in court. According to Fang Chen, the child was born to Zhou and Zhang in Xinglongfang, Danshui Road. In August of that year, he attended the baby's first-month party. In December, he heard Zhang say that she had married and the child was sent to the countryside, with Zhou responsible for living expenses. In July of this year, he still saw Zhou giving money to Zhang. The amount was unknown. Liu Wu testified that he had a room in the Qinghefang brothel. In September of that year, Zhou specially brought Zhang to his place, but only for a short time. In December, Zhang married. Zhou once told him that he and Zhang had a child. He knew nothing else. The plaintiff, Zhang Zhuying, then presented a gold ring engraved with the defendant's name and the defendant's given name, saying that it was a love token given by the defendant. The court immediately showed the ring to Zhou and asked if it was a token of love and whether the testimony of the two witnesses was true. Zhou still insisted on denying everything, saying that the testimony of the witnesses was not credible and that the gold ring was not given by him. He requested that the plaintiff's current husband be summoned to court to investigate who Dayuan was born to. The plaintiff's lawyer applied to have the defendant released on bail, saying that the defendant was addicted to smoking and feared that the case would be established, making it difficult to bear criminal responsibility. Recently, it was heard that he intended to leave the area before the verdict. If this were to happen, execution would be difficult. Therefore, he requested that the defendant be released on bail. Judge Wu ruled that the defendant had appeared in court twice and did not need to be released on bail, and ordered that witnesses be summoned for further questioning.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities

Inspects Rickshaws Operating in the Special District

1,254 Vehicles Fail to Meet Standards

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities, considering that there were many dilapidated rickshaws operating in the Special District, which were detrimental to public health and the safety of travelers, and that citizens and foreigners alike were complaining, decided to conduct an inspection. The inspection began on November 6th of last year in the open space on Qingyun Road, Zhabei. A total of 9,990 rickshaws operating in the Special District were inspected (the original number of rickshaws operating in the Special District was 10,000, but the Municipal Council of the Special District revoked the licenses of 10 rickshaws, resulting in a shortage of 10 vehicles). Among them, 1,254 vehicles failed to meet the standards. In terms of all vehicles, most had tattered canopies, followed by those with supporting iron that was too long, too short, or weak. As for the body, only a few had been rebuilt as new cars. As for those with various parts of the body that were old and tattered, requiring repairs, the number reached 525. There were also many with loose and skewed springs. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities conducted this inspection for two months, completing it on January 6th of this year.

Aviation Brand Thermos Bottles Made in China

Warmly Welcomed by Overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia

Not only is the temperature accurate and the style exquisite, but the quality is also solid, surpassing foreign products in every aspect. Therefore, since its launch, it has been widely known and warmly welcomed by overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. Orders have poured in, and there has been almost a shortage of supply. The huge sales volume has truly opened a new record for the domestic thermos bottle industry. It is heard that in order to prevent counterfeit products from appearing on the market, the factory has obtained special registration with the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and has obtained the exclusive right to use the trademark.

The Moonlight Grand Theatre Under Construction

Mr. Wang Yongmei, a real estate tycoon, is an enthusiastic participant in social undertakings. He designed and founded the Moonlight Grand Theatre on a self-owned site in Taiping Bridge, French Concession, and hired the movie and drama tycoon Mr. Li Yuanlong as the manager. The construction has been going on for several months. It is now learned that the architectural style of the theater is purely three-dimensional style of 1934. The facade and floor are the first to use bakelite, which is a new record in the history of architecture. The entire theater has more than 1,100 seats, all using spring silk sofas. It uses hot water in winter and air conditioning in summer. It is equipped with the latest "Simplex" projector and the "Altec Lansing" giant real sound sound machine, which are the same as those used in leading theaters in the city. The interior decoration is designed by art experts, and it is as luxurious as possible, costing more than 500,000 yuan. It is a rising star in the movie theater industry this year. The selection of films is balanced between Chinese and foreign. Contracts have been signed with several famous film companies. Mr. Wang and Mr. Li, based on their experience, have determined the policy of "Magnificent architecture, modern era", "Luxurious aristocratic decoration", "Line-dense scientific management", "Low seat price, popularization". Therefore, it can be truly called "Shanghai's popular film palace". It will be completed and opened in two months. At that time, Taiping Bridge will be even more prosperous.

Fourth Banks Joint Treasury Issuance Reserve Report

The 214th Time

The Fourth Banks Joint Treasury is jointly established by the Yienyieh, Kincheng, Continental, and China & South Sea Banks to handle the issuance of banknotes for the China & South Sea Bank. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with a full reserve, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a security reserve of up to 40%. A public announcement is made weekly, and it is audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 214th public announcement of the Shanghai Reserve on February 3, 1933, is recorded as follows: The amount of banknotes in circulation is 28,385,137 yuan. The total amount of reserve funds is 28,385,137 yuan, including a cash reserve of 22,052,837 yuan and a security reserve of 6,332,300 yuan.

Letter Received

To the Editor: After reviewing the news column of your newspaper on the 7th, which was headlined "Deng Darong Admits to Embezzlement and Misappropriation" and its content, it stated that the defendant admitted without hesitation to the points of embezzlement alleged by the plaintiff and the amount of misappropriation. This is slightly inconsistent with the facts. The defendant Deng Darong has appointed this lawyer as his defense counsel. I have a relatively close hearing of Deng Darong's statement. According to Deng Darong's statement, he only admitted to forging seals and defrauding funds from the Central Bank without hesitation, and did not admit to embezzlement. Although this should also be considered a criminal act, the legal penalties are very different. For the sake of the defendant's interests, I hereby request your newspaper to make a correction to avoid confusing the public. Sincerely, Lawyer Wang Siji, February 7th.

Reading Q&A

On Learning Languages ​​(Continued 2)

The letter says: "I hope to be able to understand all the ancient books," so we also disagree with memorizing ancient texts. Because my country's ancient books are vast and complex, and still need to be sorted out, beginners cannot read them, cannot finish reading them, and will become more confused as they read, so how can this help our actual lives? This is one reason. Second, the reasons for not understanding an ancient book can be roughly divided into two types: one is the lack of understanding of the text (reading ancient books requires not only understanding the organization and syntax of the article, but also studying the meanings of words and phrases), and the other is the lack of understanding of the content (such as philosophical and classical meanings). To understand ancient books, one must first seek to understand the text, but it is not uncommon for the text to be clear sentence by sentence, but the content of the article is completely incomprehensible. Therefore, reading ancient books requires more than just understanding the text; the cultivation of other knowledge is also necessary. For example, if you cannot understand new poems, it is probably not because you do not understand the sentences, because the sentences in new poems in "modern times" are not so strange. The main reason is probably that you cannot understand the "meaning" or "consciousness" contained in this type of poem. One era has the consciousness of that era, which is a natural principle. And words and language are tools for expressing consciousness. Once consciousness changes, the tools must also change—old tools cannot express new consciousness. This is not only the case in terms of word usage, but also in terms of article organization and expression. Yan Jidao used ancient Chinese to translate "The Wealth of Nations," and his ancient Chinese skills were very good, but he still felt constrained. For the sake of the text, he changed or altered many of the original meanings of "The Wealth of Nations," and could not express them very accurately and freely.

We have discussed a lot in principle, and now we will answer the five questions you asked:

(1) This is not a problem. Judging from the letter you wrote, although the article cannot be said to be very good, it is also very smooth, so your wish is not extravagant.

(2) Opinions differ on reading materials for beginners in ancient Chinese. We believe that Yao Nai's "Ancient Chinese Prose Lexicon" can also be used as reading material. But it is best to read dozens of carefully selected articles from "Kaiming" and "Beixin" by heart, and the foundation of ancient Chinese will be sufficient. As for advanced studies, one must trace back to the "Masters" and the "Two Hans"; "Master History and Classics." However, you really should not waste this energy today.

(3) We cannot determine which type of writing you should do. It depends on your own wishes, or which type of article you are willing to write. However, in the beginning, you should write more narrative prose, preferably in vernacular Chinese. Because this is the foundation of writing.

(4) We do not know the details of the Commercial Press Correspondence School. You can ask it for a copy of its charter and ask people who are familiar with its content.

(5) We cannot answer this question, because we do not know what kind of books you want to read. However, in our opinion, modern Chinese youth, regardless of their wishes, should read some books on social science common sense. Because humans are social animals, we must have a correct understanding of this society in order to adapt and survive.

In short: We have two fundamental propositions on studying languages, namely (1) we should read modern texts and (2) we should also strive to expand our knowledge. Because understanding modern texts is in line with actual life, and it will not take much effort to read ancient texts and ancient books in the future. Or it may be easier than starting with ancient texts. All learning requires going from shallow to deep, and the things that are closer to our living environment make us feel more interested, so no matter what subject the reader is reading, we advocate that he start with modern times. Expanding knowledge is even more necessary, because now many people cannot write, and they often think that it is because the words cannot express their meaning. In fact, most of them do not have systematic thoughts, in other words, they have nothing to express. A so-called article is an expression of an organized thought, and naturally fragmented and trivial ideas cannot make an article. Therefore, even a person with good writing skills, such as a essayist, cannot write an economics article (if he has no knowledge of economics at all). Even if he does, it will certainly not be a good article, because the goodness of an article does not depend solely on the goodness of the sentences and rhetoric!

Therefore, we hope that all those who study writing will not forget the principle that writing is a tool for conveying thoughts. A poor foundation in writing certainly lacks a means of expressing one's opinions; but having the skills of a tool without the tempering of thought cannot produce a good article.

Spring and Autumn

Pseudo

— Zhanlu

The lead type in the typesetting room is also changing with the surging tide. The words "Feng Zhang" and "Re Tang", which used to be connected into articles and occupied an important position on the first page of the newspaper, have now become historical terms and will no longer be found in the newspaper! In the past, the word "pseudo," which was not often used in the typesetting room, is now very busy. There is no day in the headlines that this word "pseudo" does not show up and show its face; however, the more the word "pseudo" appears in the newspaper, the more unstable the situation feels, and the general newspaper readers feel more and more headache and a variety of indescribable pain!

The pseudo-country outside the pass has been playing a puppet show for two years; recently, it has intensified, and it will be transformed from the pseudo-Manchukuo to the pseudo-Manchu Empire; from the pseudo-ruler to the pseudo-emperor; from the pseudo-Datong reign to the pseudo-Yi reign; therefore, there are related pseudo-provincial systems, pseudo-official positions, and pseudo-declarations, as well as all kinds of pseudo-things; one pseudo after another has been very troublesome for the typesetter, and it does not stop there.

The pseudo- outside the pass is causing a lot of trouble; in the communist areas inside the pass, there are pseudo-governments, pseudo-military division commanders, and all kinds of pseudo-terms appearing; the pseudo- in the communist areas has not yet been completely washed away, and in the Minbian incident, a large number of pseudo-things were produced; the Minbian has been put down, and Sun Dianying has a rumor of organizing a pseudo-Ningxia provincial government; the typesetter has just removed the words pseudo-people's government, and the words pseudo-Ningxia provincial government will replace it! Why is it that the word "pseudo" is so popular in the newspaper?

If this trend continues, the word "pseudo" in the typesetting room will inevitably "demand more than supply" and feel a shortage; it will be necessary to add more "pseudo" characters! It will be necessary to melt down the lead type that was often used in the past but is not often used now, and recast a large number of "pseudo" characters! Although we common people should not be too pessimistic about the situation, we should cling to optimism in the midst of the unoptimistic. What kind of optimism? I only hope that the word "pseudo" in the typesetting room will henceforth be "supply more than demand" rather than "demand more than supply," which is the optimism of us common people.

Casual Notes on Wooden Clogs

— Wu Jiren

Travelers have been away from home for a long time, and the teacher's term is very short. For ten years, I have not been able to visit my ancestral tomb, and my heart is full of shame. In winter, I received a report from a fellow clan member that the tomb path of Dai in Weiting was shrouded in mist, and the descendants had neglected to sweep it for many years. Some bad people had risen up and cut down ancient trees and stolen tomb fields. I was greatly frightened when I heard this. Although I had to deal with affairs in Shanghai and the vacation was short, I had to take a day off to invite my two uncles, Ding and Kun, my brother Chongwei, and my wife Fuji to brave the wind and snow, take a small boat, and sail to Jinji. The wind was strong and the sails were broken, and we were in danger. I recalled that I used to accompany my late father, visiting once a year, in a light boat, the water was calm, the shadows were dim in the third or fourth month of spring and the eighth or ninth month of autumn, the weather was clear and warm, and the wind was warm. Now it is very different. Moreover, in the fragrance of water and clouds, there is something worth savoring. The uncles and aunts sang and responded to each other, and the atmosphere was full of interest. Although I was young at the time, I also knew to listen quietly, and I learned a lot of new things. How could I have expected that the wonderful gathering would not last long, and that I would only be able to pursue it today? Now, the trees on my late father's tomb have grown, and some of my uncles and aunts are disabled due to illness, or have encountered obstacles and cannot return. My third and fourth cousins have passed away one after another. Thinking of this, how can I not secretly want to cry? There is a saying that there is a small change in five years and a big change in ten years, which is indeed true.

Yangcheng is vast and boundless, with sails dotted everywhere, and distant trees form smoke. It is the place of origin of the hairless crabs, which are famous far and wide. To the right is Jinji Lake, which is the main road to Wei. I have heard from the elders that in the late Yuan Dynasty, Jin Wushu was defeated and trapped here. The water army had thousands of people and was about to run out of food. They were surrounded by enemies on all sides, afraid of the pursuing soldiers, and had no way to resist the battle. They would definitely be defeated, and they would die if they defended. There was no way to escape. In desperation, he made an agreement with the water army that if they could dig a huge lake overnight and release the boat to run to Taihu Lake, they would have a chance to live, otherwise they would die together. Everyone followed his advice. At dusk, the soldiers each held a dustpan and worked together. By the time King Guhu was completed, they were able to escape. Later generations named it Jinji. It is a mistake to call it Jinji now.

Jinji is connected to the Shahe pond, and it is a convenient route to Taihu Lake. The area of the Shahe pond is vast, the water color is yellow and turbid, and there are waves as high as a foot, which makes it difficult for boats to travel. The Suzhou gentry Lü Gong spent private money to hire stonemasons to build a stone embankment in the Jinji Shahe pond to isolate it, which slightly reduced the water势. The embankment is thousands of feet long, solid and outstanding, and has remained intact for hundreds of years. People appreciate it. They built a monument to Lü Gong in front of the embankment to praise his great virtue, and named the embankment Lü Gong Embankment.

Bamboo fences and thatched huts, the sounds of chickens and dogs, are the joy of the farming family; the clear water mirror, a flat boat and fishing, are the joy of the fishing family. After traveling in the countryside, I often think of buying a few acres of land, building a few houses, and reading and practicing quietness in between, without honor or disgrace, and without competing with the world. Is this the peach garden of the people who avoided Qin? I will seek it in my dreams.

Bad Play

— Zhu Sizhong

A burst of erhu music was blown over by the gentle breeze, followed by the Beijing tune that sounded like a broken bamboo tube throat. Oh! What is this? I opened my legs and ran over to take a look, only to find that it was an old couple from Jiangbei, performing their bad play at the corner of the Chen's house.

The man put on a beard like a tassel of corn silk and wore an embroidered hat that no one wanted to exchange for candy. The woman also wore a flowered hat found in the trash can. One pulled, one sang, the man sometimes picked up a tree knife with the tin foil peeled off and danced wildly in the air, chanting in his mouth...Qi Bei...Qi Qi Bei.... This is probably their economic method, because hiring an extra handyman would of course cost more, so they only asked Qingzuier to help, acting as a percussionist, anyway, everything is for him.

"Shameless things, only Jiangbei people can do this kind of ugly trick." An old man with gray hair, holding a water pipe, walked over, puffing and puffing, and said this when he saw it.

"Qiaodi! Let's go, I'm afraid they'll be collecting money in a while." A taller girl gently patted the shoulder of a shorter girl and said this, and then they left together.

"Please help, it's hard for people to go out, please give me a little reward." The Jiangbei woman wearing a flowered hat held a broken wooden plate and collected money from the audience. However, the general audience looked at each other, some wished they could escape, and some stretched out a hand into their pocket, but couldn't get it out for a long time. After the woman repeatedly begged, for a full half an hour, she still couldn't collect two or three hundred yuan.

The old Jiangbei couple, sighed a few times, and threw the broken hats in the broken basket and walked away dejectedly.

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Fourth

Drinking Wine and Passing Food, Merry Partying, Containing Farewell Tears

Picking up the Lamp and Warming the Dream, Singing Softly, Passing the Long Night

He smiled and said, I just discussed with my mother that we should have a farewell party for you. Ziqiang laughed: What a joke, we're family, what farewell party? And I'll be picking you up to Qian'an soon. I've heard that our army will be transferred back from Xifengkou and stationed in Qian'an County. Guizhi walked closer, holding the corner of the table with one hand, looking at him, smiling slightly: You've said these two sentences more than twenty times. Ziqiang laughed: Really? I don't feel like it. Guizhi took another step closer, leaned against him, and looked at his face: What do you want to eat? Bao Jiao (pronounced dumplings), Chang Mian, fried meat pies, I can make them all. I'll make something for you to eat today as a farewell party. Zhao Ziqiang took Guizhi's hand and gently pressed his hand against his face, then tilted his head and looked at him: Are you not sad? Guizhi smiled: Do you think I'm a child and don't understand anything? We should be happy during our honeymoon, what's the point of being sad? Ziqiang said: What about your old lady? Guizhi smiled: My old lady is even more sensible than me, what's the point of being sad? Tell me, do you want to eat dumplings or meat pies? As she spoke, she held Ziqiang's two hands and shook them a few times. Ziqiang stood up, pressed her shoulders with his hands, and then smiled, as long as you make it, everything is delicious. Guizhi leaned into his arms and reached out to stroke his face: I'll make lamb and cabbage filling pancakes for you, okay? Ziqiang said: Good, but it's too much trouble. Guizhi said: No, I have to make filling pancakes for you to eat. Ziqiang said: Why do you have to make filling pancakes for me? Guizhi smiled and said, There is a saying that filling pancakes will not fall from the sky, probably filling pancakes are the best things. I'll make filling pancakes for you to eat today, so you can have a good sign. Ziqiang laughed loudly, and the couple had a great time in the room. (241)

Small Gardening

Winter Solstice Pure Offerings

— Holding to the Buddha

Spring days are filled with blossoming flowers and trees, while winter days are frigid, with all trees withered and fallen. However, maples and nanmu trees, having endured frost, adorn the snow with their red leaves, resembling spring flowers. Moreover, there are still a few old trees and several pots of winter plants, uniquely outstanding, bravely competing in beauty against the cold. Are they not winter month beauties and snow-bound gorgeous ladies? Hiding them in the warm room and displaying them in the study is truly a delightful companion amidst the bitter cold.

(1) Narcissus is a renowned flower in spring bonsai, with a graceful and elegant bearing, its delicate veins conveying affection. It only needs to be planted in a water jar, accompanied by clear, pure pebbles, without the need for filthy soil or foul fertilizer. It truly possesses a noble character unmatched by other plants. The ethereal goddess of the Luo River, the Han woman who unfastened her jade pendant, and the Xiang River goddess descending upon the shore are all reflections of its image. It is a perennial herb with green, slender leaves with parallel veins, and its underground stem is bulbous. As mentioned in the "Comprehensive Flora," "the root resembles a garlic bulb," which refers to the underground stem. Several flowers bloom at the top of the stem, as large as hairpin heads, botanically called umbel flowers. They are mostly white, with a separate yellow cup-shaped corona. Sun Qi's poem states, "Vanishing all icy hearts, a hint of pink." This shows its simple yet charming and cold beauty. Huang Shangu's poem states, "Containing fragrance, pure of form, about to captivate the city; the mountain alnus is its younger brother, and the plum is its elder brother." Because it blooms after the plum blossoms, it allows the plum to be the elder brother. In the past, Emperor Tang Minghuang gifted his third concubine, Lady Guo of Guo, with twelve pots of red narcissus, the pots made of gold, jade, and seven treasures. This was not only showing favor to Lady Guo but also affection for the narcissus. A Tang dynasty poem states, "Lady Guo received the Emperor's grace, riding into the palace gate at dawn; the earth disdained the rouge and powder that stained her color, she lightly swept her eyebrows to face the Emperor." It turns out that Lady Guo was a narcissus flower.

(2) Winter sweet was originally called "Yellow Plum," but it is not a species of plum. Because its flowers bloom similarly to red plums in shape and fragrance, it is called winter sweet. It is also not because it blooms in the twelfth lunar month, but because its petals resemble wax twists, so it is called "wax plum." Winter sweet is prized for its fragrance. Huang Shangu's poem states, "The body is perfumed with mountain umbilical cord, the color dyed with rose dew." Han Zicang's poem states, "Entering your house, a hundred steps of fragrance, glimpsed through the curtains, a first attempt at Han Palace makeup, one suspects dreaming of Zhaoyang Palace, a cluster of light red amidst pale yellow." The "Comprehensive Flora" states, "The fragrance of winter sweet can only be smelled from afar, not from close." It turns out that its fragrance is too strong, which is harmful to the brain. Inserting winter sweet into a gallbladder vase and displaying it on the desk, with the light dots of wax pellets and the rich fragrance of plum, is truly a fine winter offering.

(3) Heavenly bamboo is an evergreen shrub, often planted in gardens. The stems are smooth and delicate; the leaves are pinnately compound; the flower axis grows at the top of the stem. Small white flowers bloom in summer with five petals, and the fruits resemble sunflower seeds, turning red in autumn and winter, like beads, very beautiful. Planting heavenly bamboo in pots or gallbladder vases to adorn the furnishings of a small study is very elegant, is it not?

(4) Plum blossoms bloom before all other flowers and are the first to bloom in the new year. People appreciate their "color" and "fragrance"! Therefore, they have always been popular. Lin Hejing regarded it as his wife, which shows Mr. Lin's fondness. "Sparse shadows slant across the clear, shallow water; a subtle fragrance floats in the twilight moon" are also famous lines by Mr. Lin. Du Gongbu's poem states, "Walking around the eaves, I seek to laugh with the plum blossoms; the cold buds and sparse branches can barely endure." Besides red and white, there is also a type of plum blossom called "green calyx," which is mentioned in the "Stone Lake Plum Blossom Catalogue," saying that pure green plum blossoms are called "green calyx." In fact, white plum blossoms have a slight green tint when they bloom, so they are called "green calyx plum." The ancients valued horizontal, sparse, old branches, and strange forms. Nowadays, bonsai plum blossoms are twisted and sparse, possessing beauty but not from nature, so they cannot be called noble. The Book of Song says, "Emperor Wu's daughter, Princess Shouyang, was sleeping under the eaves of Hanzhang Hall. Plum blossoms fell on the princess's forehead, forming five petals that could not be brushed away. The Empress kept them. Since then, there has been 'plum blossom makeup.'" This story is very charming, and we need not concern ourselves with whether it is mythical or not. There is another myth that is also very fragrant and beautiful. Longcheng Record states, "During the Kaihuang era of the Sui Dynasty, Zhao Shixiong was traveling in Luofu. At dusk, he saw a beauty in light makeup and plain clothes welcoming him by an inn beside a forest. Shixiong spoke with her, and her words were extremely clear and beautiful, with a fragrant scent. He went to the inn with her to drink, and a green-clad boy danced by their side. Shixiong fell asleep drunk. After a long time, the east was already white. He got up and saw that he was under a large plum blossom tree, with green feathers chirping on it, the moon setting and the stars scattered. He was only filled with regret!" Looking at this myth, Zhao Shixiong seems far inferior to the reclusive Mr. Lin. Are the "understanding flowers" all superior to others?

Shenbao National Products Weekly

Housewives and Preparing for the New Year

— Yang'an

The unbreakable habit, the annual Lunar New Year's Eve, is once again upon us. Although this Lunar New Year has nothing to say about value, it has a profound relationship with the promotion of domestic goods, especially since this responsibility rests in the hands of the housewives of each family.

Recently, the busiest people in society, apart from general stores that do business, are the housewives in households. If you have the time, please pay attention to the shops on the streets. Among the customers, seven or eight out of ten are ladies and grandmothers who come to prepare for the New Year. Occasionally, some servants come to patronize, but they also come at the command of the ladies and grandmothers. Why do they come to patronize? It is to prepare for the New Year. New Year goods are a general term. Analyzed, there are about four types:

(1) Those prepared for personal use during the New Year. Such as thanking the gods for the year, celebrating the festival, worshiping ancestors, and hanging portraits.

(2) Those for entertainment during the New Year. Things for children to wear and eat, things for children to play with, and entertainment for family members themselves.

(3) Those for gift-giving. Close relatives and friends give gifts to each other, seemingly following etiquette and being unable to avoid customs.

(4) Taking advantage of this New Year, discarding old items and buying new supplies to signify a fresh start. These four types include things to eat, wear, live in, and everything used and played with. Therefore, housewives are extremely busy. However, before housewives prepare for the New Year, I want to say a few words impolitely. Since you already know that this year is the Year of National Goods for Women, then when purchasing New Year goods, be sure to pay attention to whether the New Year goods you buy are domestic goods? Are there things from foreign countries? I want to advise you to pay close attention, choose carefully, and you must know:

(1) Buying foreign goods for your own use is the most undignified thing to do.

(2) Buying foreign goods for children to eat is the most inappropriate education.

(3) Buying foreign goods to give to relatives and friends is looking down on relatives and friends, and despising their personality.

(4) Buying foreign goods for decoration is making yourself ugly and will inevitably be despised by relatives and friends.

(5) Buying foreign goods to entertain guests is despising guests and lowering their status (entertaining guests with foreign cigarettes and foreign alcohol is the most unaspiring thing to do).

I hope that wise housewives and gentlemen who love their housewives will, during this time of preparing for the New Year, just put in some effort, make a wish, patronize domestic goods factories and domestic goods companies as much as possible, hold on to the mentality of not buying anything but domestic goods, and persuade their husbands, who in turn encourage their wives. Only then will Chinese domestic goods have a chance to succeed, and foreign goods will have a hope of disappearing. I do not want to see the following two dishonorable and unlucky news items again:

(1) International Trade Bureau Report: Last year, the import quantity of cosmetics in Shanghai reached 1.4 million yuan.

(2) International Trade Bureau Report: Last year, the import quantity of foreign cigarettes and foreign alcohol had a total value of over 10 million gold yuan, with Shanghai's consumption accounting for one-third.

Talks on National Goods

The Problem of Dumping of Enemy Goods During the Year of National Goods for Women

— Huang Xuanwan

From the past of history, we can examine and review that the problem of "dumping of enemy goods" has long become the most painful page in our modern history, and its seriousness is only increasing and deepening, without any chance of resolution. Although in the middle, there was still a small change, because of the national crises of "September 18th" and "January 28th", it prompted the vigorous development of our boycott of goods movement, which was able to slightly restrain its traces. However, the cunning Japanese are not willing to give up, letting go of this piece of fat meat without firmly cutting it. Simply drooling is useless, so they will "deliberately plan", they will "rise from the ashes", they are both "colluding with unscrupulous merchants and recklessly dumping" and "disguising themselves and deceiving the people". As a result, in the end, we failed again. According to customs reports, the huge number of enemy goods imported last year was over 200 million yuan, and the four northeastern provinces under its threat are not included. The hateful enemy showed a hideous smile, but when we looked back at our domestic goods industry, the enthusiastic hope was shattered by the painful reality. However, starting from this year - the beginning of the Year of National Goods for Women, this is unanimously acknowledged by the public, and it is the most serious transition period for our domestic goods industry. What we expect from it is great and huge. However, the first voice at the beginning, when the sound of the "Year of National Goods for Women" really filled the country, the remnant sound of this "dumping of enemy goods" rose up again, separated by a distance. The prominent headline on the newspaper, "Dumping of Enemy Goods in North China is Getting Worse", they are also using organized and planned strategies to carry out large-scale dumping, and at the same time, enemy goods are becoming more and more enthusiastic throughout the country, which really has the feeling of "the mountain rain is about to come and the wind is filling the building". What is even more ridiculous is that recently, Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota, in his foreign policy statement, even expressed his coordination with China. Undoubtedly, this is another cunning means of his, a prelude to dumping during the opportunity. "Sima Zhao's heart is known to everyone", this is not surprising.

So, in this bleak charcoal painting, can we not deeply feel that the performance of this painful fact is really because our old people are too uncompetitive, and the future of the domestic goods industry is even more full of thorns and hidden reefs. This serious situation is waiting for us to open up and deal with. In my humble opinion, the measure to deal with the symptoms should pay attention to the implementation of the following two items:

1. Special Commissioners Investigate and Conduct On-site Propaganda: Domestic goods manufacturers should urgently send special commissioners to various places to conduct detailed investigations into the truth of enemy goods dumping, and conduct on-site propaganda, in order to awaken the people and make domestic goods have a trend of expansion.

2. Quickly Impose Dumping Tax: Imperialists originally took my country's low and light tariffs as the initial convenience for dumping. However, at this time, our authorities should urgently and strictly impose dumping taxes to show resistance and to give domestic goods protection.

As for the fundamental problem, naturally, as long as all the people of the country are unanimously mobilized to "regard enemy goods as floods and fierce beasts, and firmly refuse", then the rampant enemy goods, I think one day will be silenced and disappeared by the voice of domestic goods.

The Real Modern Woman

— Ba Ling

Modern woman, what a beautiful term. All women want to be modern women, who doesn't want to be a modern woman, everyone takes being a modern woman as an honor, and being called a modern woman is the ultimate glory. Modern woman! You are truly an enviable term!

What is a modern woman? How can one be worthy of being called a modern woman? According to what most people say, a modern woman must wear foreign goods, wear foreign socks and foreign shoes, have a foreign hairstyle, and everything must use foreign goods. Such a woman is a modern woman. In fact, this kind of behavior and this kind of concept are really a big mistake. In this Year of National Goods for Women, we must stand up and correct it.

In recent years, the decline of our Chinese national power and the economic depression of society are facts that no one can deny. There are certainly many reasons for this, but the economic aggression of imperialists is one of the main reasons. According to a report from the International Trade Bureau last year, the total trade deficit for the year was about 900 million yuan. Ah! This "900 million yuan" is such an alarming number! On average, each of us had to contribute two yuan to foreigners last year alone. Readers, try to close your eyes and think, can you not feel pain? Can you ignore it indifferently? In this 900 million yuan trade deficit, we can boldly say that women are responsible for six or seven tenths of it. Therefore, it has a very deep and painful meaning that this year is officially designated as the Year of National Goods for Women!

Women, stand up! In this Year of National Goods for Women, we must work hard to correct all the mistakes of the past, especially the psychology of worshiping foreign goods and using foreign goods as modern women, and we must fundamentally eradicate it. In this year, those who can implement the following articles are the real modern women.

(1) Do not say that foreign goods are good, (2) Do not buy foreign goods, (3) Use domestic goods and local goods, (4) Help the production of domestic goods.

Commemorative Paintings with National Salvation Significance

Yesterday, while the reporter was passing by Penglai Road in Xiaoximen, he saw dozens of people surrounding and watching in front of the northern window of the China Enamel Factory in the northern part of Penglai Market. No wonder his fellow villagers (Nanxiang) all gave him the nickname "Iron Abacus". Behind it, a soldier knelt next to the gun mount to aim. In front was a Chinese tank, about three feet long, with a rice bowl as the top, a tea jar as the lamp, and a top bowl basket cover as the wheel, with a small flag hanging on it, which was very lifelike. There was a Japanese plane hanging in the air. In the center, a fortress was stacked with spittoons. Outside the fortress, Chinese and Japanese soldiers were fighting hand-to-hand, with blood flowing like a stream. At first glance, it was completely a tragic picture of Zhabei. I hope to quickly practice the four characters of spiritual unity to work hard against foreign countries.

Up and Down, Ancient and Modern

— Qiacheng

(1) Introduction

Promoting domestic goods is not about talking more, but only about acting vigorously! Some say it is a year of slogans, some say it is a year of catchphrases, but we don't have to argue with people's ambitions, practical results are better than eloquent arguments, who dares to deny the real achievements. Ladies and misses, are you right?

(2) Reviving the National Spirit

Because of frequent foreign troubles, the objective environment makes us determine that we need to revive our national spirit, but national self-confidence is absolutely necessary. Although we don't have to have thoughts of arrogant self-importance, we must at least not be superstitious about others.

(3) Please See It This Way

Some people misunderstand that using domestic goods is not modern. In fact, modern is just a concept for everyone! If you think this is modern, he thinks this is also modern, fortunately there is no written law, and the expectations of the public will not succeed?

(4) Treat Domestic Goods as Children

Sons are one's own good, regardless of gender, and the same feeling is shared. Dr. Ge Chenghui humorously said that pure domestic goods are just some little treasures: I hope that ladies will treat domestic goods as children, and under the supervision of these many nannies, they will achieve great development.

Confucius discussed filial piety and said that it is all about exerting one's heart! In fact, the only principle is that everyone is clear of their conscience, exerting as much effort as they can, and it is already immeasurable merit.

National Compilation and Translation Bureau's January

Review of Primary and Secondary School Textbooks

The results of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau's review of primary and secondary school education subjects in January are recorded below.
